# Progress tracker

Tracks feature units per the workflow in `CLAUDE.md`. One section per unit.

> **Older history is archived.** Units before Spec 21 live in [`progress-archive.md`](progress-archive.md), kept out of this file to save context. This file holds Spec 21 onward.

---

## Spec 174 тАФ project Google-Maps link (precise pin) (2026-06-22)

Operator: "Add Pinned map, or attach link from gMap." Chose (one question)
**attach a gMap link** тАФ paste the Maps "Share" URL on the project; the тУШ sheet's
"open in Maps" link opens the EXACT pin, replacing the spec-173 address-search
fallback. (Embedded pinned map declined тАФ needs an API key + coordinates.)

**SHIPPED to prod 2026-06-22.** **mig 20260798:** `projects.gmap_url` (nullable) +
CHECK https-only; DROP+CREATE `update_project_settings` with a trailing
`p_gmap_url` (mirrors site_address: null preserves, '' clears) + re-applied EXECUTE
grants. **mig 20260799:** grant SELECT on the column тАФ `projects` has COLUMN-level
SELECT grants (budget excluded), so the new column did NOT inherit SELECT; granted
authenticated + anon (mirrors site_address). **mig 20260800:** revoke anon EXECUTE
on the recreated RPC тАФ Supabase default privileges silently re-granted anon EXECUTE
on the DROP+CREATE'd function; the pre-174 RPC had anon revoked (pgTAP 32 pins it).
App: `validateGmapUrl` (https + Google host allowlist тАФ rejects javascript:,
non-https, look-alike domains, >2048); the form gains a URL field; `gmapUrl` rides
the single settings payload; the project detail page computes
`mapsUrl = gmap_url ?? address-search ?? null` for the existing тУШ link (no
component change). **LESSONS (both caught by db:test, fixed forward):** (1) a new
column on a column-SELECT-granted table does NOT inherit SELECT тЖТ must grant
explicitly; (2) DROP+CREATE of an RPC re-triggers Supabase's default-privilege
EXECUTE grant to anon тЖТ must revoke anon (CREATE OR REPLACE would have avoided
both, but a new param forces DROP+CREATE). pgTAP 32 (+3, 11-arg sig); unit
validateGmapUrl + settings-form (+1 each). db:types regenerated (signature change).
Verify: db:test 120 / 2301 / 0; pnpm test green; lint┬╖typecheck┬╖build green. Builds
on [[spec173-procurement-project-visibility]].

## Spec 173 тАФ procurement read-only project visibility (2026-06-22)

Operator: "Procurement needs to see Project information and schedule." Clarified
(two questions): besides the schedule, procurement also needs the deliverables
(р╕Зр╕зр╕Фр╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ) list, to open WP details, and the project info fields (team, PM, dates,
Google-Maps link, address, status). Audit: procurement already reads /projects +
/projects/[id] + the тУШ sheet (spec 102), but a spec-102 early-return branch gave
it a minimal names+status WP list, and `deliverables` / `work_package_dependencies`
/ `project_members` SELECT had no procurement arm тЖТ empty р╕Зр╕зр╕Ф grouping, empty
schedule swimlanes/deps, empty team list.

**SHIPPED to prod 2026-06-22.** **U1 (RLS, mig `20260797000000`):** procurement
OR-arm added to `deliverables` + `work_package_dependencies` SELECT (kept the
`can_see_project` / `can_see_wp` predicate тАФ files 70/73 pins hold) and appended to
the flat `project_members` staff role-list (team-name resolution; project_director
kept, file 91). Read-only widening, no write arm. New pgTAP file 173 (+12):
procurement reads cross-project р╕Зр╕зр╕Ф + dependency + members; a membership-scoped PM
still sees only its own; quals still name the helpers. **U2 (schedule):** new
`SCHEDULE_VIEW_ROLES` (= SITE_STAFF + procurement, coordinator still excluded per
spec 154) gates `/projects/[id]/schedule` + the calendar chip (`canOpenSchedule`).
**U3 (WP nav):** `canOpenWp` re-expressed as `WP_DETAIL_ROLES.includes(role)` so
procurement's WP rows link to the (read-only, spec 171) detail. **U2+U3 removed the
spec-102 procurement early-return branch** тАФ procurement now flows through the main
project page, every write affordance already `isPmRole`/`isManagerRole`-gated and
`WorkPackageList` role-agnostic (procurement gets the р╕Зр╕зр╕Фр╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ lens by default).
**U4 (project info):** the тУШ `ProjectInfoButton` sheet gains р╕кр╕Цр╕▓р╕Щр╕░ (status),
р╕Бр╕│р╕лр╕Щр╕Фр╕Бр╕▓р╕г (start + planned-completion dates, formatThaiDate), and a р╣Ар╕Ыр╕┤р╕Фр╣Гр╕Щ Google
Maps link derived from `site_address` (no geo columns тЖТ address search URL); status
is always present so the sheet always renders. New const unit-tested
(`SCHEDULE_VIEW_ROLES`); ProjectInfoButton test extended (+2). Verify: db:test
**120 files / 2298 / 0**; pnpm test green; lint┬╖typecheck┬╖build green. RLS-only
migration тЖТ db:types regen skipped. Out of scope: project reports/settings/budget
(stay PM/super/director; budget admin-only), any procurement WRITE, geo/embedded
map, coordinator schedule access (spec 154 preserved). Builds on
[[spec171-procurement-purchase-requests]] [[spec172-procurement-back-office-domains]].

## Spec 172 тАФ procurement owns contractors / equipment / DC onboarding (2026-06-21)

Operator: "procurement also takes care of 1. Contractors 2. Equipment Rentals 3. Onboarding DCs." Decisions: FULL ownership (procurement **sets DC pay rate** +
**manages contractor bank**), build all three. **Phase A (equipment) = ALREADY
ENABLED, no-op:** audit found procurement already gated into every equipment
surface (registry CRUD/movements/rates/rental-batch+allocation+usage RPCs +
/equipment via EQUIPMENT_MOVE_ROLES/BACK_OFFICE_ROLES, spec 141/146). The only gap
is app-wide (no UI to view/manage rental batches+allocations) тАФ a SEPARATE feature,
not a procurement-permission item. **Phase B (contractors incl. bank) SHIPPED to
prod (commit 8f431bc, mig `20260795000000`):** procurement now curates contractors
like suppliers тАФ RLS adds procurement to contractors INSERT/UPDATE; CREATE OR
REPLACE `set_contact_bank` (staff bank-write) + `set_work_package_contractor`
adding procurement, **bodies sourced from the LIVE prod definition** (project_director
rides along, file 91). App: `/contacts/subcontractors` + the back-office branch of
`/contacts/[type]/[id]` (contractors+suppliers) gate on BACK_OFFICE_ROLES;
createContractorRecord/updateContractorRecord/setContactBank тЖТ backOfficeSession;
the PM-only detail workflows (bank-change approval, doc upload, portal invite,
consent) gated to isPmTier so procurement gets a clean read+bank surface without
broken affordances; `contact_bank` stays zero-grant (admin-read behind the gate).
Nav (the spec-171-U4 lesson): subcontractors added to PROCUREMENT_HUB_NAV (desktop)

- a `role==='procurement'` /settings block (phone path). pgTAP 24 (+3) / 45 (+1) тАФ
  procurement creates/updates a contractor, sets its bank, assigns it to a WP;
  db:test 0 failures; lint┬╖typecheck┬╖build green. **Phase C (DC onboarding incl.
  rate) SHIPPED to prod (mig `20260796000000`):** the concurrent spec-170 worker
  session had settled (origin/main at the Phase B docs commit, tree clean, no fresh
  worker commits), so Phase C built cleanly. CREATE OR REPLACE on `create_worker` /
  `update_worker` / `assign_worker_to_project` / `create_worker_invite` /
  `set_worker_day_rate` adding `procurement` to each role gate тАФ **every body
  re-sourced from the LIVE prod definition** (pg_get_functiondef), signatures
  UNCHANGED so the authenticated-only EXECUTE lockdown (pgTAP 36) is preserved and
  db:types needs no regen; project_director rides along in every list (file 91).
  Bank/tax/phone/day_rate are written through these definer bodies (zero
  column-grant bypassed); the READ path stays admin-only тАФ this opens onboarding,
  not PII. App: new `WORKER_ROSTER_ROLES` (= PM_ROLES + procurement) gates
  `/workers`; nav wired (the spec-171-U4 lesson) тАФ р╕Чр╕╡р╕бр╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ тЖТ `/workers` added to
  PROCUREMENT_HUB_NAV (desktop) + the `role==='procurement'` /settings block (phone
  path). New pgTAP file 172 (+19): procurement creates a DC (arrangement+bank+rate),
  updates, sets the rate, assigns to a project, issues an invite; bank/tax/phone/
  day_rate still 42501 to a raw authenticated SELECT (PII isolation preserved);
  visitor still refused (negative control). db:test 119 files / 2286 / 0; unit
  WORKER_ROSTER_ROLES (+3); lint┬╖typecheck┬╖test┬╖build green. Built via explicit-path
  commits + `push origin HEAD:main` (rebase on non-ff); never `git add -A`.
  **Spec 172 COMPLETE (A no-op ┬╖ B + C shipped).**

## Spec 171 тАФ procurement can make purchase requests from the WP screen (2026-06-21)

Status: **U1 + U2 COMPLETE тАФ shipped to prod 2026-06-21.** Operator: "there are
times procurement needs to make a purchase request instead of the site admins тАФ
enable them to see [the WP] just like site admins, but only able to edit the PRs."
Clarified: procurement **opens the work-package screen** read-only, only the
request is editable. Requests are created only in WP context (`work_package_id`
NOT NULL); that screen was `SITE_STAFF_ROLES`-gated (procurement excluded, spec
70). procurement is **cross-project** (spec 102 / ADR 0056) тЖТ `can_see_wp()` is
false for it, so it could neither read the WP's photos/labour/approvals (pure
`can_see_wp` SELECTs) nor insert a request (the INSERT also gates on
`can_see_wp`). **U1 (migration `20260780000000`, commit af754b9):** added a
`current_user_role() = 'procurement'` arm BESIDE the existing `can_see_wp` arm on
`photo_logs` / `labor_logs` (staff) / `approvals` SELECT and on the
`purchase_requests` INSERT policy (DROP+CREATE in place, names unchanged тЖТ files
70/73 `can_see_wp` pins hold). No UPDATE (can't approve/decide), no other writes;
column-scope INSERT grant already to `authenticated`. **Bug caught by db:test +
fixed-forward:** the PR-insert arm named `project_manager` without
`project_director` (I copied the role list from the pre-director migration file,
not the live post-director policy) тЖТ pgTAP file 91 "no RLS policy names
project_manager without project_director" failed; added `project_director` and
re-applied the policy to prod. **TDD:** file 17 E.6 flipped (procurement INSERT
`throws 42501` тЖТ `lives_ok`); new file **115** pins the four arms (procurement +
can_see_wp present). **db:test 115 files / 2201 / 0.** db:types = no drift (RLS
only). **U2 (commit e378d30):** admit procurement via `WP_DETAIL_ROLES`
(SITE_STAFF_ROLES + procurement) + `isReadOnlyWpViewer(role)` (the single
read-only flag the page branches on); photos render the read-only `PhaseGallery`
(extracted from /review into `components/features/photos/phase-gallery.tsx`,
behaviour-preserving) not the capture zone; labour `locked + showFlags=false`;
notes static; site-purchase / contractor-assign / assign-prompt / report-defect
suppressed; р╕Ир╕▒р╕Фр╕Бр╕▓р╕г stays planner-only. **TDD:** role-sets.test.ts pins
WP_DETAIL_ROLES + isReadOnlyWpViewer (RED first). lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ vitest 201 /
1336 ┬╖ build green. **U3 (commit 1a990be):** added `procurement` to `contractors`
SELECT (mig `20260781000000`) so the WP's assigned-contractor name shows in
procurement's read-only info sheet тАФ contractors is global master data (plain
role-level read, like the suppliers master); no app change (page already renders
it read-only). file 115 +1, db:test **115 / 2202 / 0**. **U4 (commit 9776c38) тАФ
the "procurement still can't access WP details" fix:** root cause was
NAVIGATION, not permission тАФ spec 102's separate read-only procurement project
view rendered WP rows as plain cards (no link), predating U2's read-only detail
access. Made each row a `<Link>` to `workPackageHref`; no DB change. Landed amid a
concurrent payroll/DC-payment session ([[concurrent-session-hazard]]): shared HEAD
was on its feature branch + its WIP left the tree mid-compile, so the one-file fix
was committed in isolation and ff-pushed to main (their branch/tree untouched).
**Editing an existing request's content is out of scope** (no such feature for any
role тАФ site admins only create).

Tightened `ACCOUNTING_ROLES` [accounting, pm, super, director] тЖТ **[accounting, super_admin]** (auto-tightens all 4 /accounting route guards тАФ PM/director now bounce) + gated the settings р╕Бр╕▓р╕гр╣Ар╕Зр╕┤р╕Щ тЖТ р╕Ър╕▒р╕Нр╕Кр╕╡ link to ACCOUNTING_ROLES (р╕Др╣Ир╕▓р╕Ир╣Йр╕▓р╕З/payroll stays under isManager). Reversible (re-add the 2 roles тЖТ link + guards follow). **TDD:** RED first тАФ role-sets.test.ts pins `ACCOUNTING_ROLES === [accounting, super_admin]` (+ not-contains pm/director). **Verify:** lint┬╖typecheck┬╖**vitest 200/1324**┬╖**build green** (no db:test тАФ no DB change). **Money-surface audit result: Nova operator-only тЬУ ┬╖ GL now operator-only for beta тЬУ ┬╖ project/WP pages leak no money тЬУ тАФ core-ops beta surfaces are money-safe.**

## Spec 164 U3 - bulk р╕Зр╕▓р╕ЩтЖТр╕Зр╕зр╕Ф mapping + ungrouped funnel (2026-06-21)

Status: **COMPLETE тАФ 2026-06-21.** The biggest click-saver: map many WPs into a р╕Зр╕зр╕Ф at once instead of one-at-a-time on each WP detail. **NO DB change** тАФ loops the existing `set_work_package_deliverable` RPC (spec 155; membership-gated, PM is a member тЖТ can_see_wp passes). `assignWorkPackagesToDeliverable(projectId, workPackageIds[], deliverableId)` action (PM_ROLES gate, uuid-validate/filter, sequential RPC loop, 42501/22023 map + mid-batch "р╕вр╣Йр╕▓р╕вр╣Др╕Фр╣Й N р╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ" report). `GroupWorkPackagesSheet` (target р╕Зр╕зр╕Ф `<select>` + р╣Ар╕ер╕╖р╕нр╕Бр╕Чр╕▒р╣Йр╕Зр╕лр╕бр╕Ф + scrollable WP checkbox list, each `aria-label="code name"` + "р╕вр╣Йр╕▓р╕в N р╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ" тЖТ action тЖТ refresh; Set preserves selection order). ## Spec 161 U10 - per-project defect clawback (ADR 0060 design-rule 1) (2026-06-21)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-21.** Completes the flagged follow-up (a defect-reopen claws back). Migrations `20260773000000_coin_postings_project.sql` + `20260773000100_project_coin_clawback.sql`. **Project tag:** `coin_postings.source_project_id` (nullable FKтЖТprojects, additive); **`post_coins` gained `p_source_project uuid default null`** (DROP+CREATE тАФ a defaulted-param add via create-or-replace would make a 2nd overload + ambiguate the 4-named-arg callers; plpgsql callers bind at runtime so DROP is safe; only pgTAP 96's signature pin needed updating, calls use тЙд5 positional args). **`distribute_project_coins` now TAGS** its profit_share postings (HT cut + DC shares) with the project. **`claw_back_project_coins(p_project, p_note)`** super-only: per worker, claws `least(project's REMAINING in-tail coins [signed ╬г of the project's in-window postings тЖТ nets prior clawbacks тЖТ idempotent], worker's total `coin_unvested_balance`)` as a negative `confiscation` (reason `defect_rework`, project-tagged) + a `coin_confiscations` row; per-worker advisory lock. **VESTED coins (past the tail) + OTHER projects' coins are never touched** (the trust invariant). **DECISION тАФ manual, NOT auto-fired from spec-144 reopen:** (a) a single-WP defect auto-clawing a whole project's distribution is too blunt; (b) reopen is site_admin/PM-callable but minting/forfeiting is super-only тЖТ an auto-call hits the super gate or forces an ungated post_coins bypass. Operator claws back via this RPC (UI next). **pgTAP 110** (12: column + secdef; pmтЖТ42501; super claws P тЖТ W1 keeps other-project Q coins [500] but loses P-unvested [1000тЖТbal 500], W2 P-unvested 800тЖТ0, W3 P-coins VESTEDтЖТuntouched 2000; 2 defect_rework confiscations + 2 project-tagged confiscation postings; idempotent re-run claws 0; unknownтЖТP0001). Updated pgTAP 96 (post_coins 6-arg signature). **Verify:** lint┬╖typecheck┬╖db:test 110 files/2138/0┬╖db:types┬╖test. Lesson: adding a defaulted param to a function with named-arg callers needs DROP+CREATE (overload would ambiguate), grep the signature pins.

## Spec 161 hardening - coin-engine fixes from adversarial review (2026-06-21)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-21.** Migration `20260772000000_nova_hardening.sql` (5 create-or-replace, signatures unchanged тЖТ grants kept; behaviour unchanged for 104-108). Post-arc adversarial review (3 `caveman:cavecrew-reviewer` agents over the engine SQL + UI) surfaced three real fixes (noise filtered: negative weights impossible via `nova_dials value>=0` CHECK; "vesting locks forever" was a backwards misread тАФ tail=0 тЖТ fully vested; UI was clean). **A тАФ `settle_project`:** a MISSING `coin_multiplier` dial silently produced a NULL pool тЖТ now guards тЖТ P0001 (the dial is seeded + RPC-update-only, but a deleted dial must fail loud). **B тАФ `distribute_project_coins`:** per-worker `round()` drifted тАФ ╬г shares could over-mint or lose coins тЖТ the LAST worker (by worker_id, via `row_number()/count() over()`) now takes the **exact remainder** (`v_dist тИТ ╬г allocated`) so **╬г(minted) == pool EXACTLY**, never over-mints. **C тАФ TOCTOU race:** `redeem_shop_item`/`confiscate_coins`/`award_savers_bonus` did balance-check-then-post; two concurrent calls could both pass тЖТ overspend/double-confiscate/double-bonus. Added a **per-worker `pg_advisory_xact_lock(hashtextextended('nova_coin:'||worker,0))`** (the `log_labor_day` pattern; auto-released at commit). **pgTAP 109** (6: missing-multiplierтЖТP0001; distribute 10000 over 3 equal weights тЖТ ╬г==10000 exactly + dc_distributed==10000 + each ~3333.33 + 3 postings). **Verify:** lint┬╖typecheck┬╖**db:test 109 files/2126/0** (104-108 unchanged). SQL-only тАФ no JS/db:types delta. Lessons: per-row round() in a loop drifts тЖТ allocate the last as remainder; balance-check-then-post needs a per-actor advisory lock.

## Spec 161 U6b - saver's bonus + vesting + narrow confiscation (ADR 0060 ┬з6 + decision c) (2026-06-21)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-21.** Migrations `20260771000000_add_confiscation_coin_source.sql` (enum-add) + `20260771000100_nova_vesting.sql`. The **TRUST layer** (ADR 0061 "can't build inclusion on a currency people fear"; design-rules 1/6/7): **holding is safe.** **Vesting = time-based + external lock**, derived from posting age тАФ NO project link added to coin_postings (`post_coins` untouched). **`coin_unvested_balance(p_worker)`**: an **external** DC (contractor `dc_temporary`) тЖТ the **whole balance** locked (┬з4, generalized тАФ unlocked only when invited internal); an **internal** DC тЖТ `least(balance, ╬г positive postings within `vesting_tail_days`)` (recently-earned, still in the warranty/defect tail). **`coin_vested_balance`** = balance тИТ unvested; **`coin_spendable_balance`** = vested (so external spendable = 0). All SECURITY DEFINER + **super/director gate** (null-safe, no PM тЖТ 90/91 untouched). **`redeem_shop_item` REPLACED** (same signature, grants kept) to spend only `coin_spendable_balance` тАФ the lock is now REAL (U6a built it on the full balance). **Narrow confiscation** (decision c): `confiscation_reason` enum = `('fraud','theft','gross_misconduct','defect_rework')` тАФ the 3 gross violations + the quality clawback (design-rule 1; same mechanism, distinct reason; **no catch-all `other`** тЖТ never arbitrary) + a new `confiscation` `coin_source` (2nd sink, own enum-add). **`confiscate_coins(p_worker, p_reason, p_note)`** SECURITY DEFINER **super-only**; forfeits **only `coin_unvested_balance`** (vested NEVER touched тАФ the trust invariant); `unvested тЙд 0` тЖТ P0001 (fully-vested worker is safe); posts negative `confiscation` + records `coin_confiscations` (append-only, super-read). **`award_savers_bonus(p_worker)`** SECURITY DEFINER super-only; `bal ├Ч savers_bonus_rate`; rewards **continued holding** тАФ first bonus allowed, a later one blocked if a `shop_redemption` posted since the last `savers_bonus` (P0001 'spent since last bonus'); cadence operator-driven. **New seeded dials (PLACEHOLDERS):** `vesting_tail_days 365`, `savers_bonus_rate 0.02`.

**pgTAP 108** (25: catalog 3 derives + 2 secdef + confiscation*reason labels + coin_source has confiscation + coin_confiscations table; internal vesting [unvested 500/vested 1000/spendable 1000] vs external [unvested 800/vested 0/spendable 0]; redeem respects lock [external blocked, internal spends vested]; confiscate removes 500 unvested only [balance 1000, тИТ500 posting], fully-vestedтЖТP0001, pmтЖТ42501; saver bonus 1000тЖТ1020, spender-since-bonusтЖТP0001; pm deriveтЖТ42501). **Updated pgTAP 96** again (`enum_has_labels` += `confiscation`). **Verify:** lint┬╖typecheck┬╖db:test 108 files┬╖db:types┬╖test 188/1268 тАФ all green. **U6b spec detail authored first.** **DEFERRED (own follow-up):** per-project **defect clawback auto-wiring** (spec-144 reopen тЖТ claw THAT project's unvested profit_share) needs a project link on coin_postings + a post_coins extension тЖТ flagged, not built (U6b ships time-based vesting + the `defect_rework` reason = the manual clawback). Also OUT: external inviteтЖТunlock event, attrition-signal watchlist, worker-facing vested/locked UI. **SPEC 161 ARC COMPLETE (U1тАУU6b).** **Operator MUST calibrate before go-live:** `coin_multiplier`, `ht_cut_pct`, `level_weight*\*`, `external_factor`, `vesting_tail_days`, `savers_bonus_rate` (all seeded placeholders).

## Spec 161 U6a - Nova shop + per-item pricing + redemption (ADR 0060 ┬з4) (2026-06-21)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-21.** Migrations `20260770000000_add_shop_redemption_coin_source.sql` (enum-add, own migration) + `20260770000100_nova_shop.sql`. The coin **SINK**: per-item pricing in COINS (abstract points, **no baht peg** тАФ decision b) + the redemption (spend) path. **`shop_items`** (id/name/description/`price_coins numeric(20,4) > 0`/active/sort_order/created+updated audit cols; a point price list, **NOT money** тЖТ RLS on + SELECT granted to authenticated [a future worker shop reads it], writes RPC-only). **`shop_redemptions`** (append-only spend trail: worker/item/`price_coins` snapshot/`posting_id` тЖТ the negative posting/redeemed_by/at; **zero write grant**, super-read, **self-auditing** like post_coins). **`coin_source` gains `shop_redemption`** (the first SINK source тАФ its own enum-add migration; a redemption is a negative posting). **`upsert_shop_item(p_name, p_price_coins, p_description default null, p_sort_order default 0, p_id default null) returns uuid`** SECURITY DEFINER super-only (create when p_id null, else update; name nonblank + price > 0; audits generic `update`). **`set_shop_item_active(p_id, p_active)`** super-only toggle. **`redeem_shop_item(p_worker, p_item) returns uuid`** SECURITY DEFINER **super-only** (operator-driven for now тАФ worker self-redeem later, gift-first); worker+item exist & item active тЖТ P0001; balance тЙе price (P0001 'insufficient'); posts `post_coins(worker,'shop_redemption',-price,тАж)` (existing path, negative) + records shop_redemptions (snapshot + posting_id). **U6b narrows "balance" тЖТ spendable (vested).**

## Spec 161 U5 - coin distribution: distribute_project_coins (ADR 0060 ┬з4) (2026-06-21)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-21.** Migration `20260769000000_coin_distribution.sql`. Turns the U4b settlement **pool** into postings on the spec-160 coin ledger. ADR 0060 ┬з4: **HT takes a cut off the top** (`ht_cut_pct` dial); the **rest splits by LEVEL WEIGHT** among the DCs who worked the project (SeniorтЖТApprentice; **internal > external**; externals a **flat, level-blind** share). Formulaic from `labor_logs` (the ┬з5 anti-favoritism pillar тАФ no subjective input). **A DC's share FOLLOWS THEM across project moves** тАФ the weight reads `labor_logs` (where work was done), never `workers.project_id`. **`distribute_project_coins(p_project) returns table(ht_coins, dc_distributed, dc_count, total_distributed)`** SECURITY DEFINER ┬╖ **super_admin ONLY** (minting = peak operator authority тАФ the `post_coins`/`set_nova_dial` gate; deliberately NOT super+director like U4b settlement, because distribution REUSES `post_coins` which is super-only тАФ a definer-to-definer call resolves the original caller's role, so a director would hit 42501; null-safe `is distinct from`, **no PM ref тЖТ 90/91 untouched**) тЖТ 42501. Project exists тЖТ P0001; **must be settled** (a `project_settlements` row тЖТ else P0001 'not settled'); **idempotent** (a `project_coin_distributions` row тЖТ P0001 'already distributed'). HT cut = `pool ├Ч ht_cut_pct` тЖТ `post_coins(ht,'profit_share',тАж)`; distributable = pool тИТ cut; per-DC `weight = (external? external_factor : level_weight[level]) ├Ч days` over CURRENT (non-superseded) DC labor on the project's WPs, **excluding the HT** (no double-dip); a **window `sum(weight) over ()`** over the `weight > 0` set gives ╬гweight (ungraded `level NULL` тЖТ weight 0 тЖТ filtered, never dilutes); each DC's `coins = round(distributable ├Ч weight/╬гweight, 4)` тЖТ `post_coins(dc,'profit_share',тАж)` (source **already in the enum**, no enum-add). Records `project_coin_distributions` (project_id PK = idempotency key; coin_pool/ht_worker_id/ht_coins/dc_distributed/dc_count; **zero authenticated grant**); audits (generic `update`).

**Internal vs external** = the DC's tenure: a worker whose contractor is `contractor_subtype='dc_temporary'` is EXTERNAL; null/other contractor тЖТ INTERNAL (ADR 0060 ┬з1, the `dc_regular`/`dc_temporary` subtypes; no-contractor DC defaults internal, like `wp_economics.is_external`). **New seeded dials (decision a тАФ PLACEHOLDERS, operator must calibrate before go-live):** `ht_cut_pct 0.15`, `level_weight_senior 4 / mid 3 / junior 2 / apprentice 1`, `external_factor 1` (< every internal weight тЖТ internal > external). Externals' **invisible + lock** posture: U5 only POSTS; coins already super-only-read (externals can't see them, spec 160 U3) and the **spend lock** lands in U6b. **pgTAP 106** (19 asserts: catalog + secdef; money posture; gate super-only [director┬╖pm┬╖visitor 42501]; not-settledтЖТP0001; pool 10000, ht_cut 0.2, weights senior 4/mid 2, external_factor 2 тЖТ HT 2000 (cut only, no double-dip), senior 4000, mid 2000 [share follows them тАФ now on another project], external 2000 [flat level-blind], ungraded 0; recorded ht_coins 2000┬╖dc_distributed 8000┬╖dc_count 3; total minted = pool 10000; idempotent re-distributeтЖТP0001; unknownтЖТP0001). **Verify:** lint┬╖typecheck┬╖**db:test 106 files/2073/0**┬╖db:types┬╖test 188/1268 тАФ all green. **U5 spec detail authored first.** **NEXT = U6a Nova shop** (shop_items + redeem + 'shop_redemption' coin_source) тЖТ U6b saver-bonus + vesting + confiscation. LESSON: reuse `post_coins` from a definer needs the SAME (super-only) gate, else 42501 cascade.

## Spec 161 U4b - project settlement engine: settle_project (ADR 0060 ┬з3 model-b) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-20.** Migration `20260768000000_settlement_engine.sql` (sequenced **above** the concurrent spec 146 U3 equipment block `20260767*`). ADR 0060 ┬з3 model-b: WPs bank profit as they complete; the **whole project settles ONCE at close** тЖТ `coin_pool = ╬г banked WP profit ├Ч coin_multiplier` (U4a dial). Produces the pool **number** + a **frozen snapshot**; distribution = U5. **DECISION тАФ bank-at-SETTLEMENT with a frozen snapshot (not a completion trigger):** a completion trigger fires under whoever flips the WP status (usually a site_admin on photo-approval) and would call the super/director-gated `wp_profit`/`wp_labor_sell` тЖТ **42501**, forcing an ungated refactor of shipped U3/U3b + failing the completion tx. Instead `settle_project` is an explicit super/director action **at close** that calls `wp_profit` **in its designed caller context** (gate passes) and FREEZES each completed WP's profit into `wp_profit_bank` тАФ so post-settlement corrections can't move settled coins (U5 reads the frozen bank, never live `wp_profit`). Trade-off accepted: a correction between WP-complete and project-close IS reflected (correct); defect-rework-before-close handled naturally (a WP in 'rework' isn't 'complete' тЖТ excluded). **`settle_project(p_project) returns table(coin_pool, banked_profit_total, coin_multiplier, wp_banked_count, wp_skipped_null_budget_count, equipment_costed)`** SECURITY DEFINER ┬╖ super+director null-safe `is distinct from` (no PM ref тЖТ **90/91 untouched**) тЖТ 42501; project exists тЖТ P0001; **closed-only** (`status in ('completed','archived')`) тЖТ P0001; **idempotent** (a `project_settlements` row exists тЖТ P0001 'already settled'). Loops WPs `status='complete'`, calls `wp_profit`; **budget-NULL (profit NULL) тЖТ SKIP + COUNT** (`wp_skipped_null_budget_count`, never silently 0); else **freezes** a `wp_profit_bank` row + sums; `coin_pool = total ├Ч multiplier`; audits (generic `update`). **`project_settlements`** (project_id PK = idempotency key; coin_multiplier/banked_profit_total/coin_pool/counts/equipment_costed/settled_by) + **`wp_profit_bank`** (frozen 6 wp_profit components per WP, unique per WP) тАФ both **zero authenticated grant** (money). **Equipment gap CLOSED** by the concurrent spec 146 U3 (`wp_profit` now folds in `wp_equipment_sell`) тЖТ `equipment_costed` aggregates **true**; pool no longer provisional.

**pgTAP 104** (20 asserts: catalog project_settlements+PK / wp_profit_bank / settle_project secdef; money posture both tables; gate pm┬╖sa┬╖visitorтЖТ42501; closed project w/ WP-1 budget 5000+senior-full labor 800тЖТprofit 4200, WP-2 4000тЖТ4000, WP-3 complete-no-budgetтЖТSKIPPED, WP-4 in_progressтЖТignored, multiplier 2.0 тЖТ banked 8200┬╖pool 16400┬╖banked_count 2┬╖skipped 1┬╖equipment_costed true┬╖2 bank rows; director settles a 2nd closed project; idempotent re-settleтЖТP0001; active projectтЖТP0001; unknownтЖТP0001). **Verify:** lint┬╖typecheck┬╖**db:test 105 files/2054/0**┬╖db:types┬╖**test [vitest]** тАФ all green. **U4b spec detail authored first.** **CONCURRENCY EVENT:** the spec 146 U3 equipment session was building in the SAME tree + remote DB тАФ collided on migration version 20260766000000 + pgTAP 104, and its `wp_profit_with_equipment` REPLACE changed the foundation. Operator confirmed (AskUserQuestion) the equipment session finished тЖТ I renumbered above it (768), repaired the orphan remote `20260766000000` (`supabase migration repair --status reverted` тАФ my botched first-push left a phantom version whose create-table tx rolled back), and built ON the equipment-aware `wp_profit`. **First-RED bug:** seeded projects as 'completed' THEN inserted WPs тЖТ spec-145 trigger `P0002 cannot add a WP to a closed project`; fix = seed active, add WPs, then close. **NEXT = U5 distribution** (HT cut + level-weight split тЖТ coin_postings via post_coins). LESSON: `wp_profit%rowtype` fails (it's a fn, not a relation) тЖТ use `record`; a live concurrent session in one tree/DB = the [[concurrent-session-hazard]] (check list_sessions, renumber, migration-repair the orphan).

## Spec 146 U3 - equipment usage logs: check-out/check-in тЖТ per-WP charge тЖТ wp_profit (ADR 0055 + ADR 0060 ┬з2) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-20** (commits ba8a52d feat ┬╖ 115d6ab director-fix ┬╖ 6ed8af0 types; migrations 20260767000000тАУ000400). Spec 146 U3 detail authored first.

## Spec 161 U3b - WP profit assembly: wp_profit, materials from GL (ADR 0060 ┬з2 + ADR 0057) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-20.** Migration `20260764000000_wp_profit.sql`. Assembles the ┬з2 read `profit = budget тИТ labor_sell тИТ materials тИТ equipment`, **exposing every term** (returns table). **`wp_profit(p_wp uuid) returns table(budget, labor_sell, materials_cost, equipment_cost, equipment_costed, profit)`** SECURITY DEFINER┬╖stable┬╖pinned search_path. **budget** = wp_economics.budget (NULL until PD sets тЖТ profit NULL). **labor_sell** = `wp_labor_sell(p_wp)` REUSED (definer-to-definer: caller's role resolves so its identical super/director gate passes тАФ no re-impl). **materials_cost DERIVED FROM THE GL** (ADR 0057, NOT a re-sum of purchase_requests): `╬г(debitтИТcredit)` on `journal_lines` for the WP on WIP account **1400**, restricted to PURCHASE-sourced entries via `coalesce(orig.source_table, e.source_table)='purchase_requests'` (`left join journal_entries orig on orig.id=e.reversal_of`) тАФ **reversal-safe** (a reversal carries source_table 'journal_reversal' but copies work_package_id + swaps debit/credit, so an auto-corrected purchase nets via reversal_ofтЖТoriginal's source; verified `post_purchase_to_gl` reverse-and-reposts). **Labor also debits 1400 but EXCLUDED** (source wp_labor_costs); VAT (1300) + equipment (no WP dim) naturally excluded. **profit = budgetтИТlabor_sellтИТmaterialsтИТequipment, NULL if budget NULL.** Gate **super_admin+project_director** (no PM ref тЖТ 90/91 untouched), null-safe `is distinct from` (NULL-role denied) тЖТ 42501; unknown WP тЖТ P0001; execute revoke-public/grant-authenticated; read тЖТ no audit/enum.

**EQUIPMENT GAP (operator-confirmed via AskUserQuestion 2026-06-20 тАФ chose "build profit w/o equipment, flag it"):** investigation (Explore agent + verified by hand) found `post_rental_batch_to_gl` ([20260743000100:176-178]) posts a rental batch to WIP 1400 at **batch grain with NO work_package_id (nor project_id)** тАФ equipment cost is **not WP-dimensioned in the GL**, can't be derived per-WP today. Splitting a batch across a project's WPs needs a **business allocation rule** = a follow-up spec touching the equipment poster / ADR 0055 (operator decision). U3b does NOT improvise it (scope rule + "discovering a missing requirement mid-unit isn't license to expand"): **equipment_cost=0 + equipment_costed=false** so the omission is LOUD, never folded silently. U4 minting is blocked anyway тЖТ no payout rides on the partial figure. Profit is OVERSTATED by missing equipment until that follow-up.

**pgTAP 102** (18 asserts: catalog has_function+secdef; gate super+director read / pm┬╖sa┬╖visitor 42501; WP-A all 6 components [budget 5000┬╖labor_sell 800┬╖materials 1000 (labor 1400 entry EXCLUDED)┬╖equipment 0┬╖equipment_costed false┬╖profit 3200]; WP-B reversal-safe materials [2000тИТ2000+1500=1500, profit 2500]; WP-C budget-null тЖТ budget NULL + profit NULL; unknown WP P0001). Verify: lint┬╖typecheck┬╖test **188/1268**┬╖db:push┬╖**db:test 102 files/1980/0** (was 1962 тЖТ +18)┬╖db:types (`wp_profit` added) тАФ all green. **U3b spec detail authored first.** **NEXT = equipment-per-WP follow-up spec** (allocation rule, gated on operator basis) + **U4 settlement ├Ч project multiplier** (gated on utilization data for markup-%/multiplier). LESSONS: reversal entries carry source_table='journal_reversal' (not the original's) but COPY work_package_id + swap debit/credit тЖТ net via reversal_ofтЖТorig.source_table; labor + materials BOTH hit WIP 1400 тЖТ must isolate by source, not account alone.

## Spec 161 U3 - WP labor priced at SELL: wp_labor_sell (ADR 0060 ┬з2) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-20.** Migration `20260763000000_wp_labor_sell.sql`. The **novel core** of the ┬з2 profit engine тАФ `WP profit = budget тИТ (equipment + DC labor @ SELL + materials)` тАФ built as **only** the SELL-priced DC-labor term (the one number no existing fn produces; `freeze_wp_labor_cost` sums the same logs at COST). **`wp_labor_sell(p_wp uuid) returns numeric`** SECURITY DEFINER ┬╖ `stable` ┬╖ pinned search_path. Sums over **CURRENT** labor_logs (anti-join + tombstone filter, ADR 0009 тАФ mirrors the cost engine) where `worker_type_snapshot='dc'` (own labor = payroll overhead, NOT transfer-priced тЖТ excluded, as it's absent from the ┬з2 formula), valued at the worker's per-level sell rate: `(fullтЖТ1, halfтЖТ0.5) ├Ч (internal_sell unless wp_economics.is_external тЖТ external_sell)`; `coalesce(тАж,0)`. **is_external** = `coalesce((select is_external from wp_economics where wp=p_wp), false)` (no row = internal, U2 posture). **Ungraded DC тЖТ 0** тАФ the inner join to `sell_rate_table` drops a NULL-level worker, so an ungraded DC can never silently inflate profit; **decision: contribute 0, no side-effect flag** (pure read; surfacing the ungraded-DC-day count = U3b's profit struct). **Level = live grade** (labor_logs has no level snapshot; level-at-time = later refinement, noted). **Gate super_admin + project_director only** (no project_manager ref тЖТ ADR 0058 pgTAP 90/91 untouched); **null-safe `is distinct from` form** denies NULL-role/service-role (rls-self-check-coalesce trap) тЖТ 42501; unknown WP тЖТ P0001 (typo errors, never a misleading 0). Reads zero-grant money tables (definer bypasses RLS); **invoked under the caller's authed session** (real super/director JWT so current_user_role() resolves), never the admin client тАФ like freeze. Execute lockdown: `revoke all from public; grant execute to authenticated`. Pure read тЖТ **no audit, no enum-add**. **pgTAP 101** (12 asserts: has_function+secdef; gate super+director pass / pm┬╖site_admin┬╖visitor 42501; internal WP senior-full 800 + mid-half 350 = **1150**; same crew external = **1375** and `>` internal; edge WP = **290** [only junior current-half counts: ungradedтЖТ0, own-with-level excluded, superseded-old excluded, tombstone excluded]; unknown WP P0001). Verify: lint┬╖typecheck┬╖test **188/1268**┬╖db:push┬╖**db:test 101 files/1962/0** (was 1950 тЖТ +12)┬╖db:types (`wp_labor_sell` added) тАФ all green. **Spec U3 detail authored first** (like U1/U2/U2b). **NEXT = U3b** full profit assembly (subtract equipment [spec 141/146] + materials [purchasing] from `wp_economics.budget`, **reconcile to GL** ADR 0057 тАФ derive from, not a second costing path) тЖТ U4 settlement ├Ч project multiplier тЖТ U5 coin distribution тЖТ U6 shop. **Open dial (flag, not blocking):** markup % still wants real **utilization data** for a solvent default тАФ rates are editable/seeded, so the mechanism is built; operator should sanity-check sell rates vs actual billable-vs-idle DC-days before go-live.

## Spec 161 U2 - WP economic identity: budget + internal/external (ADR 0060) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-20.** Second economics unit. Migration `20260761000000_wp_economics.sql`. The WP's profit-engine inputs, isolated so **budget keeps the MONEY posture** (the profit denominator, hidden from non-HT DCs) instead of leaking through a `work_packages` column grant тАФ mirrors `wp_labor_costs`. **`wp_economics`** (one row per WP, upserted): `work_package_id` PK+FK (on delete cascade), `budget numeric(20,4)` null (тЙе0 when set), `is_external boolean not null default false`, updated_by/at. **Zero authenticated grant** (RLS on, revoke all тАФ pm/director/super read via admin client; SECURITY DEFINER setters are the only writers). **`set_wp_budget(wp,budget)`** = **project_director + super only** (the PD sets budget, ADR 0060 ┬з1; anti-favoritism root = benchmark-to-scope) тЖТ **no project_manager ref, so pgTAP 90/91 not triggered**; validates WP-exists + budgetтЙе0 (P0001); upserts budget preserving is_external; audits. **`set_wp_external(wp,bool)`** = **pm + director + super** (PM classifies; **references project_manager тЖТ director included** per ADR 0058); upserts is_external preserving budget; audits. Both audit via generic `update` action (target wp_economics, target_id=wp), no enum-add. Gates **role-only** (not membership-scoped) for v1 тАФ budget gate is see-all anyway; PM-membership on set_wp_external = later refinement. Nothing computes profit from these yet (U3). **pgTAP 99** (19 asserts: catalog table+PK+FK+cols; money posture no-auth-SELECT; set_wp_budget director+super set / pm+visitor 42501 / unknown-WP+negative P0001; set_wp_external pm sets / site_admin+visitor 42501 / unknown P0001; **upsert preserves the other column** тАФ budget=120000 + is_external=true coexist; 3 sets audited). Verify: lint┬╖typecheck┬╖test **187/1264**┬╖db:push┬╖**db:test 99 files/1936/0**┬╖db:types тАФ all green. **NEXT = U2b** (HT assignment: `projects.ht_worker_id`, one per project, PM-assigned) then **U3 WP profit engine** (reads sell_rate_table + wp_economics + labor + equipment тЖТ profit; **needs operator UTILIZATION DATA for markup % calibration** тАФ ADR 0060 open dial). **Lesson: money column on an existing table with a table-wide grant would leak тАФ isolate WP money in a separate zero-grant table (wp_labor_costs pattern).**

## Spec 161 U1 - profit-sharing economics: per-level rate foundation (ADR 0060) (2026-06-20)

## Spec 159 U1 - subcontractor vs DC terminology consistency (2026-06-20)

Status: COMPLETE (pending full-suite green + commit). Operator: "DC setting is confusing тАФ р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓/DC, р╕Чр╕╡р╕бр╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ." Root cause: **"р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓" overloaded 3 ways** тАФ (1) general WP contractor [LEAVE, operator], (2) subcontractor `category=contractor` [firm pays its own crew], (3) DC `category=dc` [PRC pays directly] mislabeled р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓ on several surfaces. **Taxonomy already exists** (`contractor_category` + `contractor_subtype` enums; Contacts tabs render DC р╕Ър╕гр╕┤р╕йр╕▒р╕Ч/р╕Ыр╕гр╕░р╕Ир╕│/р╕Кр╕▒р╣Ир╕зр╕Др╕гр╕▓р╕з) тАФ NO schema change. **U1:** SSOT `SUBCONTRACTOR_LABEL = "р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓р╕Кр╣Ир╕зр╕З"` in labels.ts; rewired the 4 subcontractor surfaces to it (contacts-tabs TAB*LABEL.contractors + CONTRACTOR_FIELDS name + addLabel; contacts/crews title+h1; contacts/[type]/[id] TYPE_CONFIG label; settings crews door label+hint тАФ kills the `р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓/DC` slash-merge тЖТ `р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓р╕Кр╣Ир╕зр╕З / DC`). DC tab/subtypes untouched (already consistent). **CAUGHT: "р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓" is a SUBSTRING of "р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓р╕Кр╣Ир╕зр╕З"** тЖТ consistency guards assert presence-of-р╕Кр╣Ир╕зр╕З / absence-of-exact-merged-string, never absence-of-р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓. **TDD:** source-guard `contact-subcontractor-label.test.ts` (SSOT value; 4 surfaces reference the constant; settings no longer has `р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓/DC`). First test wrongly asserted the literal тАФ but SSOT means surfaces hold the \_constant name*, so the guard checks constant usage (the stronger anti-drift check).

**Open questions (OUT тАФ own units):** **U2 DC-side de-р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓** тАФ labor-cost-view (`dc: "р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓"`, `р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓ (DC)`), /payroll ("р╕Др╣Ир╕▓р╣Бр╕гр╕Зр╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓"), the DC-worker **parent picker** (worker-roster-manager + workers/actions + group-workers UNKNOWN label), the DC **portal** ("р╕Юр╕нр╕гр╣Мр╕Чр╕▒р╕ер╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓"), the role label `contractor: "р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓ (DC)"` all still call a DC "р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓"; needs the operator's chosen DC-crew word (e.g. р╕Чр╕╡р╕б DC / р╕кр╕▒р╕Зр╕Бр╕▒р╕Ф DC) first. General-WP "р╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕лр╕бр╕▓" stays generic (operator).

## Spec 157 - delete an empty work package (Tier 1) (2026-06-20)

Status: COMPLETE (pending suite green + commit). ADR 0059 ┬з3. First delete path for WPs. `delete_work_package(p_work_package_id)` SECURITY DEFINER RPC: gate pm/super/**director** + `can_see_wp()`; **refuses (P0001) if ANY child exists** (photo_logs / labor_logs / approvals / purchase_requests / work_package_members / dependencies) else deletes; writes an audit_log row (event wp_deleted + code/name). Server action `delete-actions.ts` maps P0001 тЖТ "cancel instead" message; `WpDeleteControl` (ConfirmDialog, no window.confirm) in the manager-only block, navigates to /projects/[id] on success (the WP is gone тЖТ router.refresh would 404). **TDD:** pgTAP `94` (15 asserts: catalog, FK-blocks-delete, pm empty-delete+gone+audit, super+director see-all, photo/labor/PR тЖТ P0001 + survives, sa-member+visitor role-deny, non-member pm membership-deny) + vitest `wp-delete-control` (confirmтЖТdeleteтЖТnavigate; historyтЖТinline error+no-nav).

**KEY CORRECTION тАФ the FK premise was wrong.** The investigation + ADR 0059 + spec 157 claimed `labor_logs.work_package_id` was a **bare column with no FK** (orphan risk) needing an "adjacent FK migration." **It already HAS an FK** (`references work_packages(id)`, NO ACTION тЖТ blocks WP delete with 23503; migration 20260619000300 line 22). So spec 157 dropped the FK migration тАФ **one migration only** (the RPC). ADR 0059 + spec 157 amended in place with correction notes. The empty-guard is still essential anyway: without it, deleting a WP would CASCADE-delete its purchase_requests / members / dependencies (silent data loss) and abort on the append-only photo_logs/approvals triggers. LESSON: verify FK existence by reading the table migration, not a summary тАФ `references` on the column line is the FK.

**Verify:** db:push (prod) + db:test (file 94) + db:types + lint + typecheck + full test тАФ green (below).

**Open questions (OUT):** **Tier 2 cancel/restore** for WPs WITH history (`cancelled` status enum value + exclusion from lenses/progress тАФ own spec, own enum migration); cascade/bulk delete; un-delete (gone is gone тАФ that's why Tier 2 exists). **ADR 0059 ┬зConsequences "labor_logs FK debt" is now void** (FK exists).

## Spec 155 - bind a work package to a deliverable (2026-06-20)

Status: COMPLETE (pending full-suite green + commit). ADR 0059 ┬з1. Closes the gap: `work_packages.deliverable_id` was settable ONLY by the manual seed script тАФ no post-create write path, so in-app WPs were permanently ungrouped. Added `set_work_package_deliverable(p_work_package_id, p_deliverable_id)` SECURITY DEFINER RPC: gate pm/super/**project_director** + `can_see_wp()` membership (ADR 0056/0058, the reopen precedent); NULL = ungroup; a non-null deliverable must share the WP's project (cross-project/unknown тЖТ 22023); no audit (benign metadata). Server action `deliverable-actions.ts` + a manager-only `WpDeliverableControl` native-select on the WP-detail page (р╕вр╕▒р╕Зр╣Др╕бр╣Ир╕Ир╕▒р╕Фр╕Бр╕ер╕╕р╣Ир╕б + each р╕Зр╕зр╕Фр╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ); loader gained `deliverable_id`; the project's deliverables ride alongside the loader (planner-gated, no waterfall). **TDD:** pgTAP `92` (13 asserts: catalog, pm-member bind/clear, super + director see-all, cross-project/unknown 22023, sa-member + visitor role-deny 42501, non-member pm membership-deny 42501) + vitest `wp-deliverable-control.test.tsx` (renders ungrouped+each, binds chosen id, clears to null). **Verify:** db:push (prod) + db:test **92 files / 1809 / 0** + db:types + lint + typecheck green.

**Two deviations from the spec doc (both deliberate):** (1) unknown WP тЖТ **42501** (membership gate runs first; can_see_wp is false for a missing WP тАФ we don't disclose existence to non-members), NOT the doc's "false". (2) Took **two migrations** тАФ `20260753000000` (RPC) then `20260753000100` (CREATE OR REPLACE adding `p_deliverable_id uuid default null`) тАФ because supabase typegen marks a no-default arg as required non-null `string`, so the server action couldn't pass null; the default makes it optional тЖТ the house omit-to-clear idiom (set_work_package_schedule). **Lesson: a nullable RPC arg the app must pass NULL/omit needs `default null` so typegen marks it optional тАФ author it in the first migration.** Transient `cli_login_postgres` SASL circuit-breaker hit when db:push ran concurrent with db:test тАФ retry alone clears it; don't run two supabase CLI ops at once.

**Open questions (OUT):** `create_deliverable` (in-app р╕Зр╕зр╕Фр╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ creation тАФ until it ships, binding is inert on in-app-created projects); deliverable at CREATE time (extend create_work_package + add-WP-sheet picker); bulk re-bind/drag UI.

## Spec 151 U1 - lazy client bundles: defer offline-queue runner (2026-06-19)

Status: COMPLETE (U1), build-verified; **first-load delta NOT numerically verifiable in this env** (see caveat). Bundle investigation: total client JS ~542kb gz; the 125kb gz chunk = supabase-js (browser client) + zod. zod is imported ONLY by `env.ts`/`env.server.ts` (env validation at import); the browser client by 9 client components тАФ 8 route-scoped/tap-gated, but **`UploadQueueRunner` is mounted in the root `layout.tsx`**, so it drags that 125kb chunk onto EVERY page's first paint. Fix: `src/components/features/photos/upload-queue-runner-lazy.tsx` тАФ a `'use client'` wrapper that `next/dynamic`-imports the runner with `ssr:false`; layout renders the wrapper. Safe: the runner is a background drainer for LEFTOVER offline uploads (renders null unless queued; replay idempotent ADR 0039; in-page phase-uploader unaffected), so loading it a beat after hydration is harmless. Verification: lint + typecheck + `pnpm build` all green (exit 0). **CAVEAT тАФ couldn't prove the win numerically:** Turbopack's prod build emits no per-route First Load JS table, and there's no runnable app here (no auth/prod URL), so the ~110kb first-paint reduction (124kb deferred тИТ ~14kb split overhead; total bundle ticked 542тЖТ556kb because the chunk still EXISTS, just lazy) rests on the `dynamic(ssr:false)` framework guarantee, not a measurement. **Confirm on laptop:** preview + Network tab (the supabase chunk should load AFTER first paint, not block it), or add `@next/bundle-analyzer`. **Next (later, all need a runnable app to verify):** dynamic-import the 8 tap-gated uploader/sheet components per-route; Tier-2 in-page Suspense; middleware getUser; infra.

## Spec 147 U4 - DC-portal data-fetch parallelization (2026-06-19)

Status: COMPLETE. **Final unit of the waterfall-fix sweep (rank 4).** The DC self-service portal (`portal`) ran 5 fully-serial reads then own-docs + bank-present (profile -> consents -> crew -> payments-rpc -> pending-bank-change -> own-docs -> bank-present-rpc), all RLS-self-scoped. **Sweep summary (spec 147 ranks 1-4 DONE):** four detail pages converted from serial-await waterfalls to root -> Promise.all fan -> dependent tail, each via an extracted server-only loader with a RED-first concurrency test (in-flight-counter stub; passes only when the fan overlaps). Measured (U1, prod/Singapore/warm): 462ms -> 197ms, 57%. Pattern + idiom now established (`load-detail` / `load-request-detail` / `load-portal-data`). **Follow-up (NOT this spec):** ranks 5-8 (orders/[poId], deliveries/[deliveryId], schedule, projects hub) = same fix, smaller payoff тАФ new spec when wanted. Separate larger levers untouched: `<Suspense>` streaming (perceived latency), middleware `getUser` per nav, client bundle/hydration (81 client comps), infra (Supabase Pro / cold-start).

## Spec 147 U3 - request-detail data-fetch parallelization (2026-06-19)

Status: COMPLETE. Third unit of the waterfall-fix sweep (rank 3, worst ratio тАФ ~8 fully-serial hops). The request-detail page (`requests/[requestId]`) ran request -> wp -> requester name -> attachments -> signed URLs -> poRow -> po-docs -> signed URLs -> suppliers, all in series. Collapsed to root (page fetches request, keeps isValidUuid + notFound) -> one Promise.all fan (wp, display name, request attachments, poRow, po source-docs, suppliers) -> dependent tail Promise.all (the two signed-URL mints need their attachment rows). **TDD:** `tests/unit/load-request-detail.test.ts` (RED first тАФ module-missing) -> 5 cases: concurrency (max in-flight >=5; serial peaks at 1), assembled shape, requester-name fallback (name -> email -> em-dash), suppliers gated to back-office+approved, poRow=null + no po-docs when the request has no PO. **Impl:** `src/lib/purchasing/load-request-detail.ts` (`loadRequestDetail(supabase, request, { isBackOffice })`, mirrors U1/U2). Return type inferred (not an explicit interface) to sidestep the `*_attachments_current` view-row typing. **Behavior-preserving:** same queries/columns/results; attachment splits (confirmations/invoice/reference x image/pdf/link) stay in the page as pure filters. Page drops 5 now-unused imports (SupplierOption type, mintSignedUrlsForAttachments, mintSignedUrls, PO_ATTACHMENTS_BUCKET, fetchDisplayNames); isBackOffice moved above the loader call. ## Spec 152 U3 - project_director role: table write RLS (2026-06-19)

Status: COMPLETE (U3) тАФ **FEATURE COMPLETE**. Final unit: adds `project_director` to every RLS policy whose role list literally names `project_manager`. **Why it matters:** some core PM actions are direct-table writes gated by RLS, NOT RPCs тАФ most importantly **approving a work package** (an INSERT into `approvals`), so without U3 a director could not approve. Also covers deliverables/reports/work*packages/photo_logs/photo_markups/purchase_requests writes, project_members/work_package_members manage, and the master-table READS (clients/contractors/suppliers/service_providers/equipment\*/workers) that list PM directly. **Method: reconstructed the 48 policies from the LIVE catalog (`pg_policies`), appended `'project_director'::user_role` to each role `ARRAY[...]` (Postgres reverse-compiles `in()` тЖТ `= ANY(ARRAY[])`, and has no CREATE OR REPLACE POLICY, so DROP+CREATE).** Migration `20260752000000_project_director_write_rls.sql` тАФ **48 policies / 58 role lists** widened (UPDATE policies carry PM in both USING + WITH CHECK). **NOT touched:** project-scoped SELECTs (gate on `can_see*\*`тЖТ see-all for director since U1, never name PM literally); every super_admin-alone operator policy (no PM literal тЖТ no match). **Test (REDтЖТGREEN):** pgTAP`91`тАФ completeness catalog (per-field: no policy names PM without director; 48 before тЖТ 0 after), behavioural lives_ok (director inserts an approval + updates a work_package directly on an UNINVOLVED WP тАФ see-all + role), negative control (visitor still denied тЖТ 42501). No TS change. db:push applied to prod; db:test 91 files / 0 fail. **project_director is now a complete see-all project_manager: sees everything, every RPC action, every direct-table write.** Built in isolated worktree off`main`@#77.

## Spec 152 U2 - project_director role: RPC action gates (2026-06-19)

## Spec 147 U1 - WP-detail data-fetch parallelization (2026-06-19)

Status: COMPLETE. First unit of the waterfall-fix sweep (ranks 1-4). My first "~100-200ms/hop" guess was refuted; warm hops are cheaper, but the parallel win (~halves DB time) is real and bigger in absolute terms on the full page. **TDD:** `tests/unit/load-work-package-detail.test.ts` (RED first тАФ module-missing) -> 4 cases: concurrency (in-flight-counter stub; max >=5, a serial waterfall peaks at 1), assembled shape, wp=null on project mismatch, planner-gated reads. **Impl:** extracted `src/lib/work-packages/load-detail.ts` (`loadWorkPackageDetail`, mirrors `fetchLaborZoneData` spec 46) тАФ root wp fetch -> one Promise.all fan (contractors, approvals, requests, planner-pair, labor, photos, defect) -> dependent tail Promise.all (displayNames needs approvals+requests; signedUrls needs photos). **Behavior-preserving:** same queries/columns/results, only scheduling changes. ## Incident: AppSheet EMAXCONNSESSION (2026-06-11)

Operator screenshot: AppSheet app failed to load тАФ 'max clients reached in session mode, pool_size: 48' on projects + users reads. Diagnosis: AppSheet data source pointed at the SESSION pooler (5432, per go-live checklist Step 2 wording); Supavisor session pools are per-DB-user with a 48-client cap, and AppSheet's parallel sync burst exhausted appsheet_writer's pool. pg_stat_activity showed ZERO held appsheet_writer backends at diagnosis time тАФ burst, not a leak; nothing to terminate; no prod change made. Fix: operator repoints AppSheet to the TRANSACTION pooler (6543). Checklist Step 2 now documents the port split (5432 = smoke ritual only). Raising session pool_size is not viable (already near the compute tier's max_connections). Open question: if AppSheet misbehaves on transaction mode (prepared-statement quirks), revisit тАФ fallback is a dedicated session pool budget discussion.

## Unit: architecture revision doc тАФ entrepreneur lens (2026-06-11)

- **Status:** COMPLETE (doc-only, advisory). Operator brief: "revise the architecture of this app; think like an entrepreneur, not just technical."
- **Deliverable:** [`docs/architecture-revision-2026-06.md`](./architecture-revision-2026-06.md) тАФ strategic assessment of the whole system by business criteria (cost/month, ops burden per change, engagement, sellability, moat).

### Key positions taken (all pending operator sign-off тАФ ┬з6 of the doc)

1. **AppSheet = rented ground.** Stop investing: cancel the unwritten ADR 0029 image bridge, build the in-app procurement surface + suppliers table instead (derive triggers are already writer-agnostic per ADR 0025; `procurement` role waits in the enum), demote AppSheet to read-only, then retire. Kills the per-schema-change operator tax, the Tier-2 write smoke, the EMAXCONNSESSION incident class, and the licence line.
2. **LINE notification outbox promoted to next feature slot** тАФ audit triggers already detect every hand-off event; they just don't deliver. Outbox table + drainer + LINE Messaging API channel.
3. **Railway retired when touched** тАФ PDF on-demand (route handler spike first) or Edge Function; end-state two platforms.
4. **Tenancy decided on purpose:** instance-per-customer for now + tenant-clean discipline + spin-up runbook; multi-tenant schema deferred until customer #2 is real.
5. Migration rehearsal stage (preview branch/scratch project) before destructive pushes; photo client-side downscale question raised; crew capability-URL uploads parked as v2 differentiator; dormant owner_id/work_package_members cleanup listed.

### Open questions

- The four ┬з6 operator decisions (AppSheet sunset, notifications next, tenancy posture, photo downscale).
- No code/schema/test change this unit; suites untouched (555 pgTAP / 283 unit as of a42f083).

### Spec 32 adversarial verification (3-lens workflow) тАФ fixes landed pre-commit

- **Blast-radius + discipline lens тАФ MAJOR, fixed:** `.env.example` shipped the two optional vars as empty assignments; dotenv loads `VAR=` as "" and `.optional()` rejects "" тЖТ every fresh "copy .env.example" local boot (and a blank Vercel value) would crash env validation at import time. Fixed both ends: `optionalNonEmpty` preprocess (emptyтЖТabsent) in env.server.ts + lines commented out in .env.example + 3 new env.test.ts cases (the existing per-var missing/empty pattern now covers the new vars).
- **Blast-radius minors, fixed:** photo_logs uploader enrichment included tombstone rows (uploaded_by = REMOVER per ADR 0015) тЖТ `.not("storage_path","is",null)`; no maxDuration on a 50├ЧN-push route тЖТ `export const maxDuration = 60`; PostgREST 1000-row cap on the uploader query тЖТ loud warn when hit (pilot volumes far below).
- **Security minors, fixed:** drain secret now compared via sha256+timingSafeEqual; LINE 5000-char text limit enforced by truncation in pushLineMessage (an oversized user comment was a deterministic 400 тЖТ burned all 3 attempts тЖТ actor-controlled notification suppression) + unit test; pgTAP file 25 hardened +11 asserts (plan 37): authenticated UPDATE/DELETE denial, anon denial, policies_are ZERO, EXECUTE denial on invoke_notification_drain for anon+authenticated (PostgREST RPC exposure pin), all four capture functions SECURITY DEFINER + pinned search_path, pr_created WHEN-guard negative, and the headline failure-swallowing posture PROVEN (outbox renamed away inside the transaction тЖТ WP write still lands, zero rows captured).
- **Discipline:** payload.ts (5th pure module) had no tests тЖТ notification-payload.test.ts added (key mapping, type-narrowing drops, malformed input); recorded here as declared addition alongside the admin.ts typing pull-in. pr_cancelled trigger breadth (anyтЖТcancelled vs spec's approvedтЖТcancelled) recorded in ADR 0037 as deliberate, with the audit-widening caveat for any future self-cancel unit.

Final suite state: 318 unit / 592 pgTAP / 27 e2e, typecheck+lint clean, drain endpoint live-probed 503 not_configured pre-activation.

## ADR 0034 amendment - atrophy model (2026-06-11)

Operator asked for hybrid pros/cons before AppSheet retirement; evidence pass (2-agent inventory) found the hybrid sounder than the architecture-revision urgency credited: AppSheet write surface = 9 fact columns on ONE table (decide/cancel/create/delivery-by-photo already in-app), derive/audit/notification triggers writer-agnostic, grid bulk-entry value unquantifiable yet (operator: "cannot determine"). ADR 0034 amended: parity build proceeds (in-app purchase/shipment form + suppliers still NEXT) but parity does NOT auto-demote тАФ both paths coexist; demotion when audit_log principal split shows in-app carrying >80-90% of fact-writes for several weeks, or on forcing event (customer #2 / next AppSheet outage). Column freeze + 3 open TODOs unchanged. Volume question converted to measurement (audit principal field) instead of a bet.

## Spec 34 - client photo downscale (2026-06-11)

Status: COMPLETE (operator phone pass = acceptance, spec ┬з3). Implements ADR 0036: the downscaled file IS the original; max 2000px long edge, JPEG 0.8; downscale is an optimization NEVER a gate тАФ every failure path (HEIC on non-Safari, decode/encode errors, toBlob null) uploads the original unchanged; small files pass through with EXIF intact (orientation correct either way: re-encode bakes orientation via createImageBitmap imageOrientation:'from-image', passthrough keeps EXIF).

Built: src/lib/photos/downscale.ts (computeDownscaleTarget PURE + preparePhotoForUpload browser seam) + photoExtToMime in path.ts тАФ RED confirmed pre-impl, 11 unit tests. Integrated in ALL THREE uploaders at the ext-derivation point (ext flips to jpeg on re-encode BEFORE path building): phase-uploader (PendingUpload now stores prepared blob + lastModifiedMs scalar тАФ no raw File in state; retries reuse prepared bytes), attachment stager, delivery uploader. No DB/storage diff.

### Adversarial verification (2-lens) тАФ fixes landed pre-commit

- Transparent PNG/WebP over the cap re-encoded onto a BLACK background (canvas default substrate under toBlob jpeg) тЖТ white fill before drawImage.
- REAL race (stager deferred mode): awaiting prepare BEFORE staging the chip meant a create-form submit during a slow phone decode flushed without the in-flight photo тАФ orphaned 'staged' chip, and a SECOND submission would have attached it to the WRONG purchase request. Fix: chips stage synchronously as 'preparing' (new status + р╕Бр╕│р╕ер╕▒р╕Зр╣Ар╕Хр╕гр╕╡р╕вр╕бр╕гр╕╣р╕ЫтАж display), prepare jobs tracked in a ref, flush() awaits outstanding prepares THEN reads a fresh items ref (the closure's items is stale after an await тАФ itemsRef pattern).
- createImageBitmap orientation made explicit (imageOrientation:'from-image' тАФ old Firefox/WebViews don't default to it); ext! assertions narrowed; stager header comment de-drifted; rounding test now exercises a genuinely fractional edge (3000├Ч1000 тЖТ 667).

Suite: 336 unit / 27 e2e green; pgTAP untouched (627). OPERATOR (acceptance): fresh camera photo on a test-safe WP тЖТ renders correctly oriented; Storage object ~hundreds of KB not MB (dashboard read-only check). Open seams: Web Worker offload (with the offline-queue spec), HEIC polyfill, quality/size UI, retroactive processing (never тАФ append-only).

## Spec 35 - offline-tolerant upload queue, WP phase photos (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator phone pass = acceptance: airplane mode -> photo -> banner -> close browser -> signal -> reopen -> photo lands). ADR 0039. A selected phase photo is never lost: persisted to IndexedDB at selection (survives crash/close/navigation, iOS + Android тАФ NO Background Sync dependency), uploads live exactly as before on good signal, global UploadQueueRunner (root layout; banner р╕гр╕нр╕кр╣Ир╕Зр╕гр╕╣р╕Ы N р╕гр╕╣р╕Ы only when items wait) drains leftovers on mount/online/visibility/event/backoff (5s┬╖2^n cap 5min).

Architecture: replay is IDEMPOTENT end-to-end so live-path/runner/multi-tab overlap is harmless BY DESIGN тАФ bytes 409 тЗТ alreadyExists тЗТ advance; addPhoto gains a 23505 replay path. Pure core (processQueue/QueueStore/classify/backoff) test-first vs in-memory store тАФ 15 unit tests; IDB store + runner are browser seams (house posture). Items NEVER auto-dropped (evidence); attempts only widen backoff.

### Adversarial verification (2-lens, verdict FAIL -> all fixed pre-commit)

- MAJOR (security): the 23505 verify originally checked id-exists only тАФ photo ids are readable role-wide, so a forged replay with a foreign photo id (e.g. a before-photo id + phase='after') would return ok AND flip the WP to pending_approval with zero after photos. Verify now requires the FULL replayed identity (id + work_package_id + phase + canonical storage_path).
- MAJOR (shared device): queue items now carry userId; the runner SKIPS foreign/ownerless items (uploaded_by is append-only тАФ misattribution is uncorrectable). Post-logout blob persistence recorded in ADR 0039 as an accepted tradeoff; discard UI = seam.
- MAJOR (live-path resilience): addPhoto invocation throw (the exact flaky-signal case) stuck the tile and ABORTED the multi-file loop (remaining files never queued тАФ silent loss) -> try/catch in insertOne + per-iteration isolation in handleFiles. Queue I/O (quota/private-mode IDB) wrapped non-fatal тАФ the safety net can't break the live pipeline.
- MAJOR (idempotency gap): live uploadOne wasn't 409-tolerant тАФ a runner/live overlap left a permanently-failing retry tile; now classifies alreadyExists and proceeds.
- Minors: banner staleness (notify after live remove; lock-unavailable branch refreshes count + short retry), pass-failure now reschedules (30s) instead of freezing, dead nowMs dep removed, projectId dropped from the persisted item (fileName kept for the discard seam, recorded), header lifecycle comment updated.

Suites: 349 unit / 27 e2e green; pgTAP untouched (627); no DB schema diff (addPhoto change is app-layer only). Open seams: reference/delivery photo queueing, manual discard UI, SW Background Sync, Web Worker downscale. OPERATOR: phone acceptance pass for specs 34+35 together (one outdoor session covers both).

## Spec 36 - iteration-9 debt batch (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE. Six carried items closed, one resolved-as-stale, zero schema diff. (1) browser.ts <Database> generic тАФ ALL three Supabase clients now typed; surfaced nothing. (2) Server-side length caps in validateCreatePurchaseRequest (item_description 500 / unit 40, test-first; the iteration-8 security minor) тАФ DB CHECKs still queued pending a prod data-length check. ## Spec 37 - offline queue for all photo kinds + manual discard (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator phone pass = acceptance, spec ┬з2). Closes both ADR 0039 seams: the loss-proof queue now covers reference attachments and delivery-confirmation photos (not just WP phase photos), and the р╕гр╕нр╕кр╣Ир╕Зр╕гр╕╣р╕Ы banner expands into a per-item list with confirm-guarded р╕ер╕Ъ тАФ the ONLY way an item leaves the queue without landing.

Architecture: QueuedPhoto generalized to discriminated QueuedUpload (phase_photo | reference_attachment | delivery_photo); bucket + metadata action follow the kind; the pure core stays kind-agnostic (runner's insertMeta dispatches). Legacy spec-35 items normalize to phase_photo on read (IDB schemaless тАФ no version bump). Both attachment actions gained the identity-complete 23505 replay (id + parent + kind + purpose + canonical path). Stager queues at runItem time (flush covers deferred mode once the parent exists); userId threaded through PurchaseRequestForm at both hosts. ### Adversarial verification (2-lens, FAIL -> all fixed pre-commit)

- MAJOR: addPurchaseRequestAttachment's status gate ran before the 23505 verify, so a replay whose insert LANDED but whose response was lost could never confirm after the PM decided тАФ the queue item retried forever for a photo that was already live. Fixed: decided-parent path runs the identity-complete existence check first (read-only); never-landed items on decided parents are refusable BY DESIGN тАФ the reference window closes at decision time (recorded in spec + ADR; discard is the designed out).
- Discard raced an in-flight pass: processQueue's put-backs could resurrect (or send) a just-discarded item. Fixed: QueueStore.has() re-checks before every put-back (pinned by unit test); confirm copy now promises only un-sent deletion.
- Shared-device hole in the NEW surface: the discard list let any device holder (incl. logged-out on /login) see and delete other users' un-sent evidence тАФ contradicting the ADR 0039 skip-foreign stance. Fixed: foreign items render read-only without fileName (р╕гр╕╣р╕Ыр╕Вр╕нр╕Зр╕Ьр╕╣р╣Йр╣Гр╕Кр╣Йр╕нр╕╖р╣Ир╕Щ тАФ р╕гр╕нр╣Ар╕Ир╣Йр╕▓р╕Вр╕нр╕Зр╣Ар╕Вр╣Йр╕▓р╕кр╕╣р╣Ир╕гр╕░р╕Ър╕Ъ).
- Deferred-mode queueing was dead code (userId never threaded to the create form) тАФ silent loss on flush-with-bad-signal survived. Fixed: userId through PurchaseRequestForm at /requests + WP page.
- Delivery failure copy said "р╕ер╕нр╕Зр╣Гр╕лр╕бр╣И" which would make users re-pick under a NEW uuid тЖТ duplicate rows when both landed. Copy now says queued-will-auto-send. a11y: role=status moved off the details element onto the count span (live region must not swallow disclosure semantics/buttons); summary marker restored.

Suites: 359 unit / 27 e2e green; pgTAP untouched (627); no schema diff. OPERATOR: the specs 34+35 phone pass extends to 37 (airplane-mode delivery photo -> banner -> reopen -> lands + auto-completes delivery per ADR 0030). Open seams: SW Background Sync, Web-Worker downscale, link-attachment queueing (deliberately out).

## Spec 42 - PWA standalone LINE re-login, iOS (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator iPhone pass = acceptance). Operator report: installed PWA loses login after logout; LINE re-login bounces through the LINE app to the system browser, session lands in the wrong cookie jar (iOS standalone jar is separate; CSRF state cookie also splits, so the browser-side callback dies oauth_failed). Fix per spec 42: disable_auto_login=true on the authorize URL for iOS standalone launches (verified against LINE Login v2.1 docs тАФ keeps the whole flow in the PWA's in-app overlay via LINE web login), CSS-toggled standalone login anchor (?standalone=1, display-mode arbitrary variants, no 'use client' тАФ ADR 0012 plain-anchor shape preserved), header logout CSS-hidden in standalone (profile-page logout stays, reachable via bottom tab). Android untested тАФ flag is iOS-UA-gated to avoid regressing the shared-jar WebAPK flow.

Test-first: 3 new route tests (tests/unit/line-start-route.test.ts тАФ env.server mocked at module level since serverEnv validates at import), 2 LoginButton tests, 1 AppHeader logout-wrapper pin. Playwright note: role-based locators ignore the display-hidden second anchor (a11y tree), so the existing e2e href pin survives untouched тАФ 8/8 auth e2e green on chromium. Suites: 368 unit / lint / typecheck green; no DB diff.

Recorded limitation + seam: LINE accounts with no registered email/password cannot complete the web login form (mitigation: browser login -> reinstall PWA; site data copies into the container at install). Real fix if it bites = one-time handoff code minting the session in the PWA via the existing generateLink/verifyOtp machinery (spec 42 out-of-scope section). Supabase inactivity timeout must stay "never" (operator check, no code). OPERATOR: iPhone acceptance pass тАФ install PWA, logout, log back in via LINE web login without leaving the app.

## Spec 43 - device-code handoff login for the installed PWA (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator iPhone pass = acceptance). Shipped 398f8da + types reconcile 1fd8df2 (typegen also caught up reap_stale_reports from spec 39); migration 20260618000100 applied via db push (dry-run showed zero drift first); pgTAP 656/656 (640 + file 28's 16). Operator hit spec 42's recorded limitation within minutes (LINE web login = QR or email/password; both unusable). ADR 0041: device-code handoff. PWA login tap -> POST /auth/handoff/start issues {state, device_code} row (login_handoffs, 10-min TTL, outbox zero-access posture) -> LINE auth with auto-login RESTORED (one-tap in LINE app) -> callback validates state against the DB row instead of the cookie (resolveCallbackFlow precedence: valid cookie always wins = browser path byte-equivalent), binds user_email + claims stash, status approved, shows return-to-app notice -> PWA polls /auth/handoff/poll, which atomically claims (approved->consumed) and mints the session onto the poll response via the ADR 0012 generateLink/verifyOtp pair - sb-\* cookies land in the PWA's own jar. Profile write parity (NULL-only + avatar refresh) runs at poll time from the stashed claims. Spec 42 items 1-2 reverted (disable_auto_login + ?standalone=1 anchor dead); logout hiding stands.

New surfaces: migration 20260618000100 + pgTAP file 28 (16 asserts), src/lib/auth/{line-authorize-url,line-token-exchange,handoff-flow}.ts (exchange/verify extracted - both callback paths verify identically), /auth/handoff/{start,poll} routes, StandaloneLoginButton ('use client' justified: fetch + window.open + poll orchestration; useSyncExternalStore for sessionStorage resume - react-hooks/set-state-in-effect rejects the mount-setState pattern, lesson banked), login page handoff=approved notice, proxy PUBLIC_PATHS +2. database.types.ts hand-extended pre-push; reconcile with pnpm db:types post-push. Suites: 395 unit / auth e2e 8/8 / prod build green / pgTAP 656. Seams: poll rate limiting, Android pass.

## Spec 44 - handoff resume hardening, iOS process death (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator iPhone re-test = acceptance). First spec-43 field test failed: row reached approved (browser success page shown) but PWA never claimed - iOS killed the backgrounded PWA during the LINE/Safari excursion and sessionStorage died with it (no resume, no poll, idle button). Client-only fix in StandaloneLoginButton: (1) localStorage + expiry stamp (line_handoff_device_code / line_handoff_expires_at, 600s = server TTL; stale stamp reads as nothing-stored in the useSyncExternalStore snapshot, clearing only in handlers - no side effects in render), (2) popup opened SYNCHRONOUSLY in the tap gesture (window.open after await can fall outside iOS transient user activation), opener nulled, navigated after the start POST; blocked popup -> same-window fallback (safe now that the code persists), start failure closes the orphan popup. Server untouched - approved rows wait the full TTL for a late claimer by design. 8 component tests (popup contract, resume, stale-stamp idle, fallback). Suites: 398 unit / auth e2e 8/8. Lesson banked: iOS standalone PWA storage assumptions - sessionStorage NEVER survives the app-switch kill; any cross-app handshake state must live in localStorage with its own TTL.

## Spec 45 - handoff opens LINE in same window, no popup (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator iPhone re-test = acceptance). Spec-44 field test: home app went ALL WHITE on tap - iOS standalone PWAs have NO tab model; the spec-44 synchronous window.open('', '\_blank') swaps the visible view to a dead about:blank and the later popup navigation never reaches the user. Fix (client-only, third round on ADR 0041): popup path deleted; tap -> start POST -> store code (spec-44 localStorage+expiry) -> SAME-WINDOW navigation to LINE (no transient-activation concern). Return trip = spec 44's resume: PWA resumes (user closes out-of-scope top-bar view) or relaunches cold at start_url; any LoginButton page resumes the poll. Cancel pin caught a REAL bug: cancel from a resumed waiting state mutated only storage (no React state delta) so useSyncExternalStore never re-read - storage mutations now emit to subscribers (proper external store, not the noop-subscribe shortcut). Suites: 397 unit / auth e2e 8/8. Lessons banked: (1) standalone PWA = never window.open, same-window nav + persistent resume state is the pattern; (2) noop-subscribe useSyncExternalStore is a trap whenever mutations can happen without an accompanying state change.

## Spec 68 - Labor P2: cost freeze, PM cost view, close-out variance (2026-06-13)

Status: CODE COMPLETE, local gates green; migration GATED on operator confirm before db:push (prod). Implements the P2 block deferred in spec 46 - cost is the Head Tech surplus-share pilot's input (CEO-review 'Now' #1, unblocked since C1-C7 were already operator-resolved). MODEL: wp_labor_costs snapshot (work_package_id PK, own_cost/dc_cost numeric(12,2), computed_at, frozen_by) - DELIBERATELY MUTABLE one-row-per-WP UPSERT (the audit_log carries the change history, so the snapshot need not be append-only; C6: a post-close labor correction never recomputes it silently - a pm/super re-freezes explicitly, audited). ZERO authenticated grant (money) - read only via the admin client behind requireRole(pm/super), like day_rate_snapshot. freeze_wp_labor_cost(p_wp) SECURITY DEFINER: pm/super gate else 42501 (site_admin refused - rate is money, like set_worker_day_rate); WP-existence probe (SECURITY DEFINER bypasses RLS); own/dc = sum(fraction x day_rate_snapshot) over CURRENT (non-superseded, non-tombstone) labor logs; ON CONFLICT upsert; ONE labor_cost_freeze audit row with own/dc + old_own/old_dc in payload. KEY DECISION: invoked via the caller's AUTHENTICATED session, NEVER the admin client - current_user_role() = role from users where id=auth.uid(), and the service-role client has no JWT (auth.uid() NULL) so the gate would 42501 it; the authenticated PM session yields project_manager + a real frozen_by/audit actor. Two call sites: AUTO in recordDecision right after the admin UPDATE flips the WP to complete (non-fatal - logs on error, never fails the approve; C6 makes a missed freeze recoverable), and the explicit refreezeWpLaborCost action behind a re-freeze button shown on drift. New audit_action 'labor_cost_freeze' in its own migration (ADD VALUE can't be referenced same-txn); enum-label pins updated in files 03 AND 18 (grep-all-pins; file 19's audit_action ref is an action='update' filter, NOT a label pin - verified, so only 2 needed this time). 2 migrations (20260623000000 add value, 20260623000100 table+RPC; RPC tightens beyond the P1 labor RPCs - revoke execute from public, grant to authenticated - since it writes money). App: pure helpers TDD-first (bangkokDateOf in dates.ts; aggregateLaborCost/findOverAllocatedDays/currentLaborPairKeys/fractionDays in labor/cost.ts; computeLaborVariance + LABOR_VARIANCE_MIN_DIFF=2 in labor/variance.ts - the SQL freeze sum MUST equal aggregateLaborCost). database.types.ts hand-extended (wp_labor_costs Row/Insert/Update + freeze fn + enum union + Constants array). UI (PM page ONLY - the SA page stays presence-only; money never on a site_admin-reachable screen): admin-client cost read; LaborCostView server component (own/DC subtotals + total baht, per-worker days+cost+self-log, C5 cross-WP >1.0/day flags filtered to this-WP pairs, frozen-vs-live drift note + RefreezeButton client child); AttentionCard amber close-out variance strip (photo-days bucketed bangkokDateOf vs labor work_dates, surfaces at symmetric-diff >=2 OR photos-with-zero-labor). Tests: 26 new unit (labor-cost/labor-variance/dates-bangkok) RED then GREEN; pgTAP file 34 (plan 20: shape/PK/RLS/zero-grant posture, role gate sa+visitor 42501, happy-path own=750/dc=380 + one audit row, WP-not-found P0001, re-freeze upsert single-row + 2 audit rows + prior 750 in payload, superseded/tombstone excluded). Local: 580 unit / lint / typecheck / prod build green; pgTAP 34 + db:types reconcile PENDING the gated db:push.
