## Spec 137 - Action-state bands + view filter on the site /requests worklist (2026-06-17)

Status: COMPLETE on prod тАФ 2026-06-17. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **995 unit** (+7 new TDD) ┬╖ green. **Operator:** site people need more than р╕Чр╕▒р╣Йр╕Зр╕лр╕бр╕Ф/р╕Вр╕нр╕Зр╕Йр╕▒р╕Щ, the flat sort "is not intuitive", and "at the very least be able to filter out items received." (I recommended + built; aligns with the locked SA action-state lens, [[worklist-priority-alignment]].) The non-procurement `/requests` view (SA/PM/super) was a flat list (pending by priority, then everything newest-first) + a р╕Чр╕▒р╣Йр╕Зр╕лр╕бр╕Ф/р╕Вр╕нр╕Зр╕Йр╕▒р╕Щ toggle. **Pure helper** `src/lib/purchasing/request-bands.ts` (7 unit tests, TDD): `requestBand(status)` тЖТ action-state band; `groupRequestsByBand(rows, view)` тЖТ ordered non-empty bands **р╕гр╕нр╕нр╕Щр╕╕р╕бр╕▒р╕Хр╕┤** (requested) тЖТ **р╕нр╕Щр╕╕р╕бр╕▒р╕Хр╕┤р╣Бр╕ер╣Йр╕з р╕гр╕нр╕кр╕▒р╣Ир╕Зр╕Лр╕╖р╣Йр╕н** (approved) тЖТ **р╕Бр╕│р╕ер╕▒р╕Зр╕Ир╕▒р╕Фр╕кр╣Ир╕З** (purchased/on_route) тЖТ **р╣Ар╕кр╕гр╣Зр╕Ир╣Бр╕ер╣Йр╕з** (delivered/site_purchased) тЖТ **р╣Др╕бр╣Ир╕нр╕Щр╕╕р╕бр╕▒р╕Хр╕┤/р╕вр╕Бр╣Ар╕ер╕┤р╕Б** (rejected/cancelled), active bands sorted priority-then-oldest (`comparePendingRequests`), done/closed newest-first; `RequestView` active(default)/done/all with `VIEW_BANDS` тАФ **active HIDES received+closed** (the operator's minimum). **Page:** `?view=` (default active); the non-procurement filter row is now a **view segmented control** (р╕Бр╕│р╕ер╕▒р╕Зр╕Фр╕│р╣Ар╕Щр╕┤р╕Щр╕Бр╕▓р╕г/р╣Ар╕кр╕гр╣Зр╕Ир╣Бр╕ер╣Йр╕з/р╕Чр╕▒р╣Йр╕Зр╕лр╕бр╕Ф) + a **р╣Ар╕Йр╕Юр╕▓р╕░р╕Вр╕нр╕Зр╕Йр╕▒р╕Щ** toggle (replaces the old р╕Чр╕▒р╣Йр╕Зр╕лр╕бр╕Ф/р╕Вр╕нр╕Зр╕Йр╕▒р╕Щ 2-chip; each preserves the other axis via `reqHref`, defaults omitted from the URL); the list renders as **band sections** (heading + count + cards), 3-way empty state (no requests / none in this view / bands). No new query (bands computed over the already-fetched pending+decided rows). **Procurement view unchanged** (keeps its spec-104 pipeline + spec-110 filters). **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated; the band helper carries the tests). Spec doc `137-site-worklist-bands.md`. Acceptance owed: site sees grouped bands, default hides received, view chips + р╣Ар╕Йр╕Юр╕▓р╕░р╕Вр╕нр╕Зр╕Йр╕▒р╕Щ work. **Consistency refinement (2026-06-17, operator: "check UI, not the same as the other side; think hard what users want to know"):** the site bands now match the procurement pipeline's section styling тАФ `hot` band (amber heading + amber count chip) where the site's attention band = **р╕Бр╕│р╕ер╕▒р╕Зр╕Ир╕▒р╕Фр╕кр╣Ир╕З** (incoming = what site receives, the analogue of procurement's buy-now band). And the thing site most wants to know тАФ **is anything late** тАФ surfaces as a `р╣Ар╕ер╕вр╕Бр╕│р╕лр╕Щр╕Ф N` danger chip on a band with overdue arrivals (`groupRequestsByBand(rows, view, today)` counts items whose `eta` < today; +3 unit tests, 998 total). The shared `PurchaseRequestCard` already carries ETA/tracker/status per row.

## Spec 95 (hardening) - iOS keyboard-freeze: scroll-independent repaint for short forms (2026-06-17)

Status: code COMPLETE, **NOT device-verified** (desktop preview cannot reproduce the WebKit/iOS-PWA quirk тАФ operator must confirm on a real iOS PWA, especially a SHORT form). **App-only, no migration.** lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **999 unit** ┬╖ green. **Operator: "fix the frozen screen after closing the keyboard for good."** Recurrence #2 of the spec-95 blank-after-keyboard glitch (recurrence #1 = the still-focused-field case, fixed 436ee6f). **Root cause:** every `ViewportScrollGuard.repaintScroller` path forced the repaint via `scroller.scrollBy(0,1)` тАФ which only repaints when `<main>` can actually scroll. A form that fits the viewport (no overflow) can't scroll тЖТ scrollBy moves nothing тЖТ the locked scroller (spec 64: body overflow:hidden, `<main>` the only scroller) stays blank. The 85% of long forms recovered; short ones froze "for good". **Fix:** `repaintScroller` now ALSO does a scroll-INDEPENDENT repaint тАФ a 1px `transform: translateY(1px)` nudge on `<main>`, restored on the next rAF (preserves any existing transform; the 1px shift is invisible for one frame) тАФ re-rasterizing the layer regardless of content height. Belt-and-suspenders with the existing scroll nudge; both the focusout (force=false, keeps the mid-edit field-to-field skip) and visual-viewport-resize (force=true, the still-focused recurrence) paths get it. TDD: 3rd test in `viewport-scroll-guard.test.tsx` asserts the transform is set inside the repaint and cleared next frame. **Verified-by-checklist** (jsdom has no layout/WebKit; the unit test pins the DOM contract, the real proof is the operator's device test). If it recurs again: next levers are lowering the 80px keyboard-down threshold, nudging on `geometrychange`, or firing across more frames of the ~250ms keyboard slide.

**Recurrence #3 тАФ "hidden, not frozen" (2026-06-17):** operator reported the prior fix didn't take and reframed the symptom тАФ the screen feels **hidden** (pushed off), not blank/frozen. That's a DIFFERENT bug than the missing-repaint one. The layout comment (`app/layout.tsx`) says the guard's job is to "snap the locked document back to top тАж (otherwise the header is pushed off)", but `git log -S scrollTo` proves the guard **never** snapped to top тАФ only the net-zero nudge ever existed, so the header-pushed-off case was unhandled the whole time. Mechanism: body is locked (spec 64 overflow:hidden) so `window`/document scroll should always be 0, but iOS pans the document up to reveal a focused field near the bottom and doesn't always undo that pan on keyboard-close тЖТ the sticky header sits ABOVE the visible viewport ("hidden"). The net-zero nudge can't fix a real offset. **Fix:** `repaintScroller` now also `window.scrollTo(0, 0)` on keyboard-close (always safe тАФ a locked body cannot legitimately scroll; does NOT touch `<main>`'s own scroll = the reading position); gated by the same force/mid-edit logic so it never yanks the viewport while the keyboard is still up. TDD: +2 tests (snaps to top on close; does NOT snap while another field is being edited). **1001 unit** ┬╖ lint ┬╖ typecheck green. **Still NOT device-verified** тАФ operator must confirm on a real iOS PWA. If still seen: the pan may be a visual-viewport offset rather than a layout scroll тЖТ next lever is also zeroing `document.documentElement.scrollTop` / handling `visualViewport.offsetTop`.

**Recurrence #4 тАФ "BOTTOM BLANK GAP" тАФ actual root cause (2026-06-17):** prior two fixes (repaint, snap-to-top) didn't take. Diagnostic questions cracked it: operator says a **blank gap at the BOTTOM** (not top, not frozen), recovered by **rotate / navigate / refresh but NOT by scrolling**. That discriminator rules out both earlier hypotheses тАФ not a paint bug (scrolling would fix it), not a scroll offset (snap-to-top didn't fix it). It's a **stale viewport HEIGHT**: iOS standalone PWA leaves the locked body/`<main>` at the keyboard-REDUCED `100%`/`h-full` height after the keyboard closes, so the vacated bottom strip stays blank; rotate/navigate/refresh fix it because they all force a fresh relayout at the restored height. **Fix:** `repaintScroller` now also pins `document.body.style.height` to the live `window.innerHeight` for one frame, then releases it back to the CSS `h-full` lock on the next rAF тАФ replicating the rotate relayout so `100%` re-resolves against the correct viewport (own rAF, restores even with no `<main>`). TDD: +1 test (pins to innerHeight, clears next frame). **1002 unit** ┬╖ lint ┬╖ typecheck green. The guard now does FOUR things on keyboard-close: height relayout (bottom gap) ┬╖ window snap-to-top (hidden header) ┬╖ scroll nudge (blank scrollable) ┬╖ transform nudge (blank short form). **Still NOT device-verified** тАФ if the bottom gap persists, escalate from the one-frame toggle to PERMANENT height tracking (set body height = innerHeight on every resize/orientationchange, the `--app-height` pattern) rather than relying on iOS to recompute `100%`.

**Recurrence #5 тАФ STOP guessing, instrument (2026-06-17):** the height-relayout toggle (#4) also didn't take on device тАФ operator: "problem still there". Three blind fixes missed because the surface is auth-gated + iOS-PWA-only (no desktop repro), so the actual stale dimension is still unknown. Switched from guessing to MEASURING: new **`ViewportDebug`** flag-gated diagnostic overlay (`src/components/features/chrome/viewport-debug.tsx`, mounted in `app/layout.tsx`) тАФ renders null unless `?vpdebug=1` (or `localStorage.vpdebug="1"`), otherwise a fixed top-left overlay printing live `innerHeight / visualViewport.height/offsetTop/pageTop / documentElement.clientHeight / body.rectH / main.rectH+clientH+scrollH+scrollTop / window.scrollY / doc.scrollTop / activeElement`, updated on resize/scroll/orientationchange/focusin/focusout (+vv resize/scroll). Operator opens the broken screen with `?vpdebug=1`, closes the keyboard, screenshots the numbers in the blank-gap state тЖТ tells us which dimension is wrong тЖТ one definitive fix instead of a 4th guess. TDD: `viewport-debug.test.tsx` (renders null without flag; overlay with flag). **App-only, flag-gated, zero impact on normal use.** lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ test green. **TEMPORARY тАФ remove once the real fix lands.** The viewport-scroll-guard fixes (#2тАУ#4) stay in (each is harmless and may help one of the sub-cases); the next fix targets whatever the device numbers reveal.

**REGRESSION + REVERT (2026-06-17):** fixes #2тАУ#4 were NOT harmless тАФ operator: the orange р╕Цр╣Ир╕▓р╕вр╕гр╕╣р╕Ы hero bar (phase-uploader, `position: fixed inset-x-0 bottom-0`, a descendant of PageShell `<main>`) was "hovering all over the screen". Cause: the #4 `transform: translateY(1px)` nudge on `<main>` тАФ a CSS transform makes the element the **containing block for its `position:fixed` descendants**, so the fixed capture bar (and any fixed chrome: tab bar, modals, toasts) detaches from the viewport and tracks `<main>`. Worse, the guard's resize path fires `repaintScroller(true)` whenever `innerHeight - vv.height < 80`, which is TRUE even with no keyboard (vv.height тЙИ innerHeight), so incidental iOS visualViewport resize/scroll events re-applied the transform constantly тЖТ the bar wandered. **Action:** reverted `viewport-scroll-guard.tsx` + its test to the last-good pre-regression commit `4b90a3a` (436ee6f baseline = net-zero `scrollBy` nudge only); dropped the transform nudge, the `window.scrollTo(0,0)`, and the body-height pin (all three unverified, all three fired on the always-true gate). **The keyboard bug itself is still UNFIXED** тАФ but the guard is back to a known-good state and the regression is gone. The `ViewportDebug` overlay (af25bc5/6253d14) stays тАФ it's a fixed top-left `pointer-events:none` box that transforms no ancestor, so it's safe тАФ and it's now the path to a real diagnosis. **Lesson:** never put a `transform` on the scroll container тАФ it reparents all fixed chrome; and the `< 80` resize gate is too loose (fires without a keyboard), so anything behind it must be a true no-op when no keyboard is present.

**Recurrence #7 тАФ THE FIX (browser-verified) (2026-06-17):** operator sent the actual screenshots. They settled it: post-revert the orange bar is correctly bottom-fixed (regression gone), and the `/requests` create form is **physically clipped at the focused field (р╕Ир╕│р╕Щр╕зр╕Щ/р╕лр╕Щр╣Ир╕зр╕в) with a giant blank gap below** тАФ the scroller is collapsed to the keyboard-reduced height, not merely unpainted. Confirms the stale-height mechanism: the locked `html тЖТ body тЖТ main` chain is all `h-full` (=100%); iOS standalone shrinks the web view for the keyboard and never recomputes `100%` on close, so the root stays short тЖТ `<main>` clipped тЖТ blank gap. The #4 one-frame toggle failed because it released back to the broken `100%`. **Fix = new `AppHeightTracker`** (`src/components/features/chrome/app-height-tracker.tsx`, mounted in `app/layout.tsx`): pins `documentElement` + `body` height to the live `window.innerHeight` and re-applies on `resize` / `visualViewport resize` / `orientationchange` / `pageshow` / `focusout`(+100ms settle), so the keyboard-close resize restores the full height for real instead of relying on iOS to recompute `100%`. `<main>`'s `h-full` follows the corrected root. **No transform** (the regression lesson) тАФ only an explicit root height. **Browser-VERIFIED in the preview** (the first fix in this arc confirmed before shipping): at 812 the tracker pins html/body/main = 812px; shrink the viewport to 500 + fire resize тЖТ all track to 500; restore to 812 + fire resize тЖТ all restore to 812 (the keyboard openтЖТclose cycle); zero console errors. TDD: `app-height-tracker.test.tsx` (pins on mount; re-applies the restored height on resize). lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **1002 unit** (147 files) green. **Still owed: operator device confirmation** on the real iOS PWA (the in-app keyboard fires the resize/visualViewport events the preview can't), but the mechanism is now proven, not guessed. `ViewportDebug` overlay stays until confirmed, then both it and any vestigial guard nudge can be removed.

**Recurrence #8 тАФ wrong API found by research; corrected to visualViewport (2026-06-17):** #7 didn't work either, and web research (martijnhols.nl OSK article, htmhell viewport guide, quirksmode) explained why: **on iOS the soft keyboard is a SEPARATE LAYER тАФ the layout viewport never changes, so `window.innerHeight` stays constant and the window `resize` event does NOT fire when the keyboard opens/closes.** #7's `AppHeightTracker` was built on innerHeight + window resize, so it literally could not respond to the keyboard. Also confirmed: `interactive-widget=resizes-content` is NOT implemented in iOS Safari, so the declarative fix is out. **The only reliable signal is `window.visualViewport`** (`.height` shrinks; the `resize`/`scroll` events fire). **Rewrote `AppHeightTracker`** to publish `Math.round(visualViewport.height)` as the **`--app-vh`** CSS variable on `documentElement`, driven by `visualViewport.resize`/`scroll` (+ window resize/orientationchange/pageshow + focusout fallbacks + a 300ms delayed re-read for iOS's close-lag where visualViewport.height doesn't settle immediately). **PageShell's `<main>`** is now `style={{ height: "var(--app-vh, 100%)" }}` (h-full class stays as the pre-JS/non-iOS fallback) тАФ so the scroller tracks the actually-visible area: it shrinks above the keyboard and restores to full on close. CSS variable only тАФ **NO transform** (the reverted regression) and no scroll change, so fixed chrome is untouched. **Browser-VERIFIED in the preview:** at 812 тЖТ `--app-vh` 812px, main computed 812px; shrink the visual viewport to 500 тЖТ main 500 (the `visualViewport.resize` listener fires automatically, unlike window resize); restore to 812 тЖТ main 812; zero console errors. TDD: `app-height-tracker.test.tsx` rewritten with a mocked `window.visualViewport` (publishes --app-vh on mount; restores on visualViewport resize). lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ test green. **Device pass still owed** тАФ the preview proves the wiring + the right API, but only the real iOS keyboard fires the genuine visualViewport events. If it STILL fails, enable `ViewportDebug` (corner├Ч5 / `?vpdebug=1`) and screenshot тАФ the live vv.height vs innerHeight numbers will confirm the model.

**Recurrence #9 тАФ THE ACTUAL CAUSE, from on-device numbers (2026-06-17).** Made `ViewportDebug` ON by default (#8.5) so the next screenshot carried the metrics. It did, and it ended six rounds of guessing. **Broken state, keyboard CLOSED (`active=body`): `window.scrollY = 389`, `document.documentElement.scrollTop = 389`** (also `vv.height=744`, `vv.offsetTop=49`, `doc.clientH=793`). The body is LOCKED (spec 64 overflow:hidden) so the document must always be at scroll 0 тАФ it was at **389**. iOS scrolls the documentElement to reveal the focused input when the keyboard opens and **does not reset it on close**, leaving the whole page shifted up ~389px = exactly the bottom blank gap. **Not paint, not main-height, not a stale 100% тАФ a stuck DOCUMENT scroll.** Every prior fix was the wrong axis; the `--app-vh`/visualViewport-height experiment (#8) even made `<main>` 49px short (744 vs the 793 layout) and is now REVERTED. **Fix:** `ViewportScrollGuard` rewritten to force `documentElement.scrollTop` / `body.scrollTop` / `window.scrollTo(0,0)` back to 0 when the keyboard is DOWN (`innerHeight - visualViewport.height < 100`, so it never fights iOS revealing the input mid-edit), fired on focusout + visualViewport resize/scroll + orientationchange/pageshow, with 300ms/600ms re-reads for iOS's late settle. Only the document scroll is touched тАФ `<main>`'s reading scroll is left alone; no transform, no height changes. Reverted: deleted `AppHeightTracker` + its test, removed it from layout, PageShell `<main>` back to plain `h-full`. TDD: guard test rewritten (resets doc scroll to 0 when keyboard down; does NOT reset when keyboard up). lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ test green; preview confirms no regression (main full height, no console errors). `ViewportDebug` stays default-on for the confirmation screenshot тАФ expectation: in the broken-flow re-test, `window.scrollY`/`doc.scrollTop` now read 0. Remove the overlay once the operator confirms.

**Recurrence #10 тАФ THE REAL ROOT: iOS auto-zoom on input focus (2026-06-17).** After the doc-scroll-reset, operator: **"zooming out to 100% solves the blank portion."** That reframes it тАФ the page was ZOOMED IN, and the `scrollY=389` pan was the zoom-pan, not an independent document scroll. Cause confirmed in code: the form fields are NOT the `ui/input` primitive (which is `text-base`=16px on mobile) тАФ they're hand-rolled `<input>`/`<select>`/`type=date`/`<textarea>` at **`text-sm` = 14px** (`purchase-request-form.tsx` lines 201/222/241/297/308/358, and the same pattern across other forms). **iOS auto-zooms into any focused input whose font-size < 16px**, and a standalone PWA leaves the page zoomed + panned after blur тЖТ the blank portion; manual zoom-to-100% clears it. **Fix (design-preserving, global):** viewport meta now `width=device-width, initial-scale=1, maximum-scale=1, user-scalable=no` (Next `viewport` export: `maximumScale:1, userScalable:false`) тАФ a standalone PWA honors it and iOS no longer auto-zooms on focus, so the field-first `text-sm` sizes stay unchanged. **Trade-off:** disables pinch-zoom app-wide (acceptable for a native-feel ops PWA; operator framed zoom as the bug). Alternative if pinch-zoom must stay: bump every form input to 16px (enlarges field text, many files) тАФ offered to operator. Verified in preview: the rendered `<meta name=viewport>` content = `тАжmaximum-scale=1, user-scalable=no`; no console errors. Added `vv.scale` to `ViewportDebug` so the operator can confirm scale stays 1.00. The doc-scroll-reset (#9) stays as defense. lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ test green.

## Spec 95 тАФ RESOLVED + cleanup (2026-06-18)

Operator confirmed on device: **no more zoom, no blank portion.** Root cause = iOS auto-zoom on `<16px` form inputs; fix = `maximum-scale=1` in the root `viewport` export (global тАФ the only `viewport` export in the app, so it covers every form on every screen). **Cleanup refactor:** removed the temporary `ViewportDebug` overlay (component + test + layout mount + corner-tap gesture); confirmed no dangling `--app-vh` / `AppHeightTracker` / `vpdebug` references remain. **Kept** `ViewportScrollGuard`, reframed as defense-in-depth for the spec-64 body-lock invariant (document scroll stays 0 if iOS scrolls the documentElement to reveal a focused input) тАФ a cheap no-op in the normal case; its header comment now points at `maximum-scale=1` as the primary fix. Browser-verified: overlay gone, viewport meta still `тАжmaximum-scale=1, user-scalable=no`, no `--app-vh` leftover, no console errors. lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ test green. The spec-95 saga (#1тАУ#10) is closed; memory `ios-keyboard-repaint-freeze` rewritten to lead with the auto-zoom root cause + the process lesson (for device-only bugs: ship a metrics overlay first, get one screenshot, then fix the named dimension). **Possible follow-up (not done, scope):** the 14px hand-rolled inputs duplicate styling across forms тАФ a shared form-field input component would centralize the size decision and document the <16px-zoom trap.

## Spec 138 U1 тАФ р╕Хр╣Йр╕нр╕Зр╕Хр╕┤р╕Фр╕Хр╕▓р╕бр╕Фр╣Ир╕зр╕Щ urgent-follow-up panel (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE тАФ 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **1003 unit** (+4 new TDD) ┬╖ green. **Source:** a Claude Design (claude.ai/design) handoff bundle ("Mobile-first redesign for tablets", primary file `PRC Ops Worklist Mobile.dc.html`) тАФ the operator mocked the desktopтЖТmobile worklist UX and asked to implement the relevant aspects. Named distinct from the existing `AttentionCard` callout primitive (different thing). **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated procurement page тЖТ no preview; the pure helper carries correctness). Spec doc `138-mobile-worklist-redesign.md` (index updated; also backfilled the missing 136/137 index rows). **Next units (not started, one-per-session):** U2 KPI hero restyle (amber-gradient р╕гр╕нр╕кр╕▒р╣Ир╕Зр╕Лр╕╖р╣Йр╕н tile + icons + tap-to-filter); U3 scrollable status-chip filter with live counts (replace the status `<select>`). **Refinement (2026-06-18, operator: "Remove р╕Хр╣Йр╕нр╕Зр╕Хр╕┤р╕Фр╕Хр╕▓р╕бр╕Фр╣Ир╕зр╕Щ section from phone view"):** wrapped the render in `hidden lg:block` so the panel now shows only on tablet/desktop (lg+) тАФ its origin in the design (the desktop `.dc.html` added it first, mobile mirrored). On the phone the р╣Ар╕Бр╕┤р╕Щр╕Бр╕│р╕лр╕Щр╕Ф KPI tile (its filter toggle) stays the chase entry point; the panel read as redundant there. className-only, no logic/helper/test change; lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ test green.

## Spec 138 U3 тАФ scrollable status-chip filter with live counts (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE тАФ 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **1015 unit** (+8 new TDD: 5 chip helper + 3 band axis) ┬╖ green. **U3 = the desktop/mobile mock's status chips.** Replaces the procurement worklist status `<select>` with a horizontally-scrollable row of BAND pills (р╕Чр╕▒р╣Йр╕Зр╕лр╕бр╕Ф / р╕нр╕Щр╕╕р╕бр╕▒р╕Хр╕┤р╣Бр╕ер╣Йр╕з=`to_order` / р╕Бр╕│р╕ер╕▒р╕Зр╕Ир╕▒р╕Фр╕кр╣Ир╕З=`in_transit` / р╣Ар╕Бр╕┤р╕Щр╕Бр╕│р╕лр╕Щр╕Ф=overdue), each with a LIVE count. **Introduces the band filter axis** the U2 seam flagged тАФ a single raw `status` enum can't express the in_transit band's purchased-OR-on_route set, so a later unit can now make the р╕гр╕нр╕кр╕▒р╣Ир╕Зр╕Лр╕╖р╣Йр╕н/р╕Бр╕│р╕ер╕▒р╕Зр╕Ир╕▒р╕Фр╕кр╣Ир╕З KPI tiles tap-to-filter (reuse this axis). **Filter axis** (`src/lib/purchasing/worklist-filter.ts`): `ProcurementFilter` += `band: ProcurementBand | null`; `matchesProcurementFilter` AND-composes it (`procurementBand(row.status) === filter.band`); `buildWorklistQuery` serializes `?band=to_order|in_transit` (between project + status). The raw `status` axis STAYS (no UI now, but `?status=rejected` still surfaces the banded-out rejected/cancelled history тАФ the only escape, kept to avoid a regression). **Pure helper** `src/lib/purchasing/worklist-status-chips.ts` `buildWorklistStatusChips({rows, filter, todayIso})` тЖТ 4 chip descriptors `{key,label,count,href,active}` in order (all┬╖to_order┬╖in_transit┬╖overdue); counts reuse the spec-105 `procurementSummary` (so they agree with the KPI hero) + `all` = rows with a non-null band; `rows` is the supplier/project-narrowed set тЖТ counts are LIVE to those axes; each `href` reuses `buildWorklistQuery` preserving supplier/project/status while setting band+overdue per chip; `active` = overdue wins, else band, else all (5 unit tests, TDD). **Component** `WorklistStatusChips` (server-safe, presentational, no `'use client'`): `overflow-x-auto` `<Link>` pill row, each label + count badge, active pill `bg-fill/text-on-fill` тАФ mirrors the spec-137 `worklistChipClass`, min-h-11 tap floor, Field-First tokens only (passes design-doctrine: no green-\*/no-min-h-9). **Page** (`src/app/requests/page.tsx`): parses `?band` (validated against `PROCUREMENT_BANDS`), builds the chips over supplier/project-narrowed rows, renders `<WorklistStatusChips>` between the KPI grid and the supplier/project pickers; `filterActive` += `filter.band`. Band filtering flows through `matchesProcurementFilter` + the existing `groupByProcurementBand` (an active band yields that one group); the `status` flat-group branch is untouched. **`ProcurementFilters`**: removed the status `<select>` (+ its now-dead `STATUS_OPTIONS` / label import / `PurchaseRequestStatus` type); supplier/project pickers stay; the р╕ер╣Йр╕▓р╕Зр╕Хр╕▒р╕зр╕Бр╕гр╕нр╕З clear-all now also resets `band`. **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated procurement page тЖТ no preview; pure helpers carry correctness; operator device/desktop look-feedback is acceptance). Spec doc updated (U3 Change section). **Open question (decided):** removing the `<select>` drops the only VISIBLE path to filter rejected/cancelled тАФ kept reachable via the `?status=` URL but no longer a control (spec-sanctioned; bands already drop those from the pipeline). **Spec 138 = U1┬╖U2┬╖U3 done.** Next possible unit: make the р╕гр╕нр╕кр╕▒р╣Ир╕Зр╕Лр╕╖р╣Йр╕н/р╕Бр╕│р╕ер╕▒р╕Зр╕Ир╕▒р╕Фр╕кр╣Ир╕З KPI tiles tap-to-filter (the band axis is now in place); sortable grid columns (care: overrides priority/PO-contiguity order).

## Spec 138 U4 тАФ KPI hero tiles tap-to-filter (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE тАФ 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **1019 unit** (+4 net: the `worklist-kpis` test rewrote from 4 тЖТ 8 cases) ┬╖ green. U4 = the final mock affordance: the р╕гр╕нр╕кр╕▒р╣Ир╕Зр╕Лр╕╖р╣Йр╕н (`to_order`) and р╕Бр╕│р╕ер╕▒р╕Зр╕Ир╕▒р╕Фр╕кр╣Ир╕З (`in_transit`) KPI hero tiles are now clickable band toggles (deferred from U2 "needs the bandтЖТstatus mapping", which U3 then built), reusing the U3 band axis. **Pure helper** (`src/lib/purchasing/worklist-kpis.ts`): `buildWorklistKpis` now takes `{ summary, outstanding, filter }` (dropped the pre-built `overdueHref`/`overdueActive` pair) and derives every tile's `href`/`active` internally via `buildWorklistQuery` тАФ mirroring the U3 `buildWorklistStatusChips` so the toggle logic lives in one place. A `bandTile(band)` helper builds the р╕гр╕нр╕кр╕▒р╣Ир╕Зр╕Лр╕╖р╣Йр╕н/р╕Бр╕│р╕ер╕▒р╕Зр╕Ир╕▒р╕Фр╕кр╣Ир╕З tiles as band toggles: `href` sets that band while clearing `overdue` (`band === key ? null : key` тАФ re-tapping the active tile clears it back to р╕Чр╕▒р╣Йр╕Зр╕лр╕бр╕Ф); `active = !filter.overdue && filter.band === key` (so neither band tile reads active while the overdue chase is on). The р╣Ар╕Бр╕┤р╕Щр╕Бр╕│р╕лр╕Щр╕Ф tile is UNCHANGED тАФ exactly the existing chase toggle `buildWorklistQuery({ ...filter, overdue: !filter.overdue })` / `active = filter.overdue` / danger-when-`overdue > 0 || filter.overdue`; р╕Др╣Йр╕▓р╕Зр╕Ир╣Ир╕▓р╕в stays static (`href: null`). **`WorklistKpiTile`: no change** тАФ its `href`тЖТ`<Link>`+pressed-ring branch (U2 built it for the р╣Ар╕Бр╕┤р╕Щр╕Бр╕│р╕лр╕Щр╕Ф tile) already covers the two new band tiles; the hot/shipping tones flow through it unchanged. **Page** (`src/app/requests/page.tsx`): passes `filter` to `buildWorklistKpis` (dropped the inline `overdueHref`/`overdueActive` args; `buildWorklistQuery` import stays тАФ the U1 panel footer still uses it); updated the stale "only the р╣Ар╕Бр╕┤р╕Щр╕Бр╕│р╕лр╕Щр╕Ф tile is a filter toggle" comment to note all three pipeline tiles toggle. 8 unit tests (TDD): order/captions, static tones, band-tile href+idle, active band toggles off, band hrefs preserve supplier/project + clear overdue, overdue chase toggle preserved, outstanding static, overdue tone. **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated procurement page тЖТ no preview; the pure helper carries correctness; operator device/desktop look-feedback is acceptance). Spec doc updated (U4 Change section + Units/Out-of-scope). **Spec 138 = U1┬╖U2┬╖U3┬╖U4 done тАФ the full mock is shipped.** Possible later unit: sortable grid columns (care: overrides priority/PO-contiguity order).

## Spec 139 U1 тАФ App-feel slice 3: optimistic worker active-toggle (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE тАФ 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **1021 unit** (+2 new TDD) ┬╖ green. App-feel slice 3 (optimistic UI) was the last deferred slice тАФ done CAREFULLY per-surface, payroll-safe only. U1 = the worker active-toggle on `/workers` (`WorkerRow` in `src/components/features/labor/worker-roster-manager.tsx`), the clean safe pick: already a client component, the toggle reads `worker.active` only for presentation (name colour, `(р╕Ыр╕┤р╕Фр╣Гр╕Кр╣Йр╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ)` suffix, button label), nothing server-computed beside it. **Introduces React 19 `useOptimistic`** (was zero usage in the codebase). **Change:** replaced the toggle's `busy` + success-only `router.refresh()` with `committedActive = useState(worker.active)` (post-mount truth, advanced only by a successful flip) + `optimisticActive = useOptimistic(committedActive, (_, next) => next)` + `useTransition` (`isToggling`). `toggleActive` is now sync: inside `startToggle(async тАж)` it `setOptimisticActive(next)` (instant flip), awaits `updateWorker({ id, active: next })`, and on ok `setCommittedActive(next)` (commit тАФ the optimistic falls through to it when the transition ends, **no `router.refresh`** тЖТ the flicker is gone), on `!ok` `toast.error(result.error)` (the optimistic auto-reverts to `committedActive` = the rollback, now explained via the slice-1 toast channel тАФ the toggle previously failed **silently**). The row renders name colour / `(р╕Ыр╕┤р╕Фр╣Гр╕Кр╣Йр╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ)` suffix / button label from `optimisticActive`; button `disabled={isToggling}` (no double-fire race). **Untouched** (out of scope): the add-worker form + per-row edit-save stay pessimistic (they surface server validation + need the new/edited row to appear тЖТ keep `router.refresh`; `useRouter` import stays); the action + RPC + page unchanged; no styling/class change (design-doctrine green). **Tests** (`tests/unit/worker-roster-manager.test.tsx`, +2): optimistic flip-before-server + commit (deferred-promise: label flips to р╣Ар╕Ыр╕┤р╕Фр╣Гр╕Кр╣Йр╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ + `(р╕Ыр╕┤р╕Фр╣Гр╕Кр╣Йр╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ)` suffix appears while pending, `updateWorker({id:"w1",active:false})`, **no `router.refresh`**; resolve ok тЖТ stays flipped); rollback + toast (`{ok:false}` тЖТ reverts to р╕Ыр╕┤р╕Фр╣Гр╕Кр╣Йр╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ, suffix gone, `toast.error` fired, no refresh). The 4 existing notes/picker tests unchanged. **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated pm/super `/workers` тЖТ no preview; the component tests carry correctness; operator on-device eyeball = acceptance, the slice-76/77/78 convention). Spec doc `139-app-feel-optimistic-ui.md` written (index row added; spec-138 index row relabelled to the full mock). **Next:** more payroll-safe optimistic surfaces (later units, per-surface); slice 5 motion (CSS list-enter via `@starting-style`; route View Transitions = guarded spike only). **Care recorded:** money/payment + labor-day logging surfaces are explicitly NOT optimistic candidates (server-computed / auditable).

## Spec 140 U1 тАФ App-feel slice 5: staggered list-enter motion (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE тАФ 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **1025 unit** (+4 new TDD) ┬╖ **build green** (CSS compiles тАФ ran `pnpm build` since CI/eslint don't cover globals.css). Pivoted to slice 5 (motion) after an investigation showed slice-3's remaining optimistic surfaces all carry desync (WP hold-status is a central field read across the page) or sensitivity (bank-change approval, consent) risk тАФ the worker toggle was the one uniquely-clean surface (operator chose the pivot). Route View Transitions stay a guarded spike (out of scope). **Pure helper** `src/lib/ui/list-enter.ts` `listEnterProps(index)` тЖТ `{ className:"list-enter", style:{"--enter-index": step} }` where `step = clamp(trunc(index), 0, LIST_ENTER_STAGGER_CAP=8)` тАФ the cap is load-bearing (a long list's tail must not wait seconds; rows past the cap share the last step), the testable seam (4 tests: index, clamp-0/negative, cap-tail, trunc-fraction, TDD). **`globals.css`** `@keyframes list-enter` (opacity 0тЖТ1, translateY 6pxтЖТ0) + `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: no-preference){ .list-enter{ animation: list-enter 240ms ease-out both; animation-delay: calc(var(--enter-index,0) * 35ms) } }` тАФ matches the spec-76 `toast-in` / spec-78 `sheet-up` pattern; `both` holds the row invisible through its stagger then settles visible; reduced-motion users get static fully-visible rows (the `from{opacity:0}` only applies while the animation is attached, which only happens inside the no-preference query тЖТ no FOUC). **`WorklistRow`** gained optional `enterIndex?: number` (merged into the root `<Link>` тАФ appends the class + sets the style var; omitted тЖТ every existing caller untouched). **`work-package-list.tsx`** passes `enterIndex={i}` from the map index at the 3 WorklistRow render sites (grouped-by-band / flat action-state / deliverable-group `<li>`) so the WP list glides in uniformly in every group mode. Server-safe (no `'use client'`; class+style are plain markup), zero data risk. **Verified-by-checklist + build** (auth-gated project page тЖТ no preview; the helper test carries the cap logic; CSS animation isn't unit-testable тЖТ operator on-device eyeball = acceptance, the slice-77 visual-slice precedent; design-doctrine green тАФ "list-enter" trips no green-\*/min-h-9 rule). Spec doc `140-app-feel-motion.md` written (index row added). **Next:** more lists (procurement worklist cards, contacts, suppliers, requests тАФ fast-follows reusing `listEnterProps`); route / View Transitions later (guarded spike, never the foundation); slice 3 optimistic continues per-surface (payroll-safe only).

## Spec 143 U1 тАФ membership-scoped project visibility (ADR 0056) (2026-06-18)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-18.** lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **1086 unit** ┬╖ green; **pgTAP file 70 green post-push (30/30; full suite 70 files / 1455 asserts, 0 failures)**; `db:push` applied `20260728000000`; `db:types` reconciled. Operator's 2nd ask: **project_manager + site_admin now see only the projects they're involved with** (a `project_members` row OR `project_lead_id`); **project_coordinator + super_admin see all**; **procurement keeps** its spec-102 cross-project read on projects/work_packages/purchase_requests. **Full RLS isolation** (operator decision) тАФ enforced on every project-scoped table, not just the hub. **ADR 0056** (amends 0013) written + indexed; spec 143 written + indexed. **Migration** `20260728000000_project_visibility_scope.sql`: two SECURITY DEFINER STABLE helpers тАФ `can_see_project(uuid)` (super/coordinatorтЖТtrue; pm/site_adminтЖТmember-or-lead; else false, never NULL тЖТ closes the [[rls-self-check-coalesce]] trap) and `can_see_wp(uuid)` (resolves WPтЖТproject, coalesce false); definer so they read project_members/projects/work_packages without re-triggering the policies that call them (ADR 0011, no recursion). **LeadтЖТmember backfill** in the same migration (idempotent `on conflict do nothing`) keeps current leads visible. **Rewrote 7 SELECT policies** (writes untouched), each preserving its exceptions: projects/work_packages = `procurement OR can_see_project`; deliverables = `can_see_project`; photo_logs/approvals = `can_see_wp`; purchase_requests = `requested_by=auth.uid() OR procurement OR can_see_wp` (separate appsheet_writer policy untouched); reports = `can_see_project AND role<>'site_admin'` (spec 19 тАФ reports still never reach site_admin). Eval-once wrapped form throughout (file 40). **Authoritative current policies pulled from pg_policies first** (not stale migration files) тАФ caught that spec 102 had added procurement to projects+work_packages. **pgTAP file 70** (plan 30): helper behaviour across 8 role/involvement combos + can_see_wp; projects/work_packages end-to-end per-row visibility (member sees, non-member doesn't, procurement keeps all, visitor none); child-policy wiring (qual references the right helper; reports excludes site_admin; PR keeps requester self-read). **Blast radius (expected тАФ access-model change):** 15 existing pgTAP suites hard-coded the old "PM/site_admin see everything" and broke on the read; fixed by seeding each fixture's PM/site_admin test users as project_members of its fixture project (scoped by test code + `auth.users.email` subquery тАФ `public.users` has no email column, the first attempt's trap). One ADR-0026 qual pin (file 17: "PR SELECT admits site_admin site-wide") was obsoleted by 0056 and re-pinned to the new `can_see_wp` gate. **No app code changed** тАФ RLS filters every cross-project list automatically (hub, worklists, payroll, reports). **ROLLOUT HEADS-UP (operator):** turning this on hides existing projects from PMs/site_admins who aren't a member/lead. Prod data is tiny (2 projects, 2 PMs, 3 site_admins; backfill enrolled the 1 lead) + super_admin sees all, so add the right people to each project via project settings (spec 80 UI). **Verified-by-checklist** (RLS is the SUT; pgTAP 70 + the regression suite carry correctness; operator on-device pass = acceptance). **Next:** U2 тАФ enable `project_coordinator` as a real role (roleHome тЖТ `/projects` + add to PROJECT_VIEW_ROLES so the see-all coordinator can actually browse; currently lands on /coming-soon). Then onboarding U5тАУU7 (WP seeding) remain.

## Spec 143 U3 тАФ complete the membership-scoping U1 missed (2026-06-18)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-18.** lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **1096 unit** ┬╖ green; **full pgTAP suite 73 files / 1489 asserts, 0 failures** post-push; `db:push` applied `20260731000000` + `20260732000000` (fix-forward, below); `db:types` reconciled. A **full-project-lifecycle audit** (4 parallel explorers) found U1's "full isolation" was incomplete: three project-scoped child tables still had role-level SELECT (cross-project leak to PM/site_admin), and the SELECT-only U1 left the app write policies role-level (a non-member could write a row for a project they can't read). **Migration `20260731000000`:** scoped `labor_logs` (staff SELECT only тАФ the bound-contractor self-read untouched) + `work_package_dependencies` SELECT via `can_see_wp`; mirrored the membership gate onto the **8 app write policies** (photo_logs INSERT, approvals INSERT, purchase_requests app-INSERT, deliverables INSERT+UPDATE, reports INSERT, work_packages UPDATE тАФ each KEEPS its role list so `project_coordinator` stays read-only; `labor_logs`/`wp_dependencies` are RPC-write-only so no write policy to mirror). Authoritative current policies pulled from `pg_policies` first (not stale files). **Self-inflicted regression + fix-forward:** `20260731000000` also tried to scope `photo_markups` (SELECTтЖТ`can_see_photo_log`, + helper). `photo_markups`' INSERT policy self-references `photo_markups` (tombstone-target EXISTS) тАФ safe only under a trivial role SELECT policy; under a function SELECT policy Postgres raised **42P17 infinite recursion** on every markup INSERT (caught by pgTAP files 31 + the test, but the migration was already pushed тЖТ prod markup-insert briefly broken). **`20260732000000`** reverts `photo_markups` to its original working policies + drops the unused `can_see_photo_log` тАФ prod un-broken. **pgTAP file 73** (plan 12): labor_logs + wp_dependencies + 7 write-mirror wirings + wp_dependencies end-to-end (member sees dep / non-member doesn't). **Two existing suites repaired:** `29-labor-capture` got a membership seed (its `correct_labor_log` id-lookup reads labor_logs as the PM тАФ now scoped); `31-photo-markups` returns to green once `photo_markups` reverted. **Verified-by-checklist** (RLS is the SUT; pgTAP 73 + the suite carry it). **Lesson:** scoping a SELECT policy on a table whose own write policy self-joins that table triggers 42P17 (ADR 0011 trap) тАФ needs a SECURITY DEFINER tombstone-target helper (pr_attachment_tombstone_target_ok precedent). **Remaining leak (documented, deferred to U4):** `photo_markups` is still role-level (low sensitivity тАФ drawing annotations). `labor_logs` (the sensitive one тАФ worker/day data) IS closed. **SPEC 143 now: U1 (RLS) + U2 (coordinator) + U3 (labor_logs/wp_dependencies + write-mirror) on prod; U4 (photo_markups via definer helper) is the one open item.**

## Spec 143 U4 тАФ scope photo_markups (recursion-free) (2026-06-18)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-18. SPEC 143 COMPLETE.** lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **1096 unit** ┬╖ green; **full pgTAP suite 74 files / 1501 asserts, 0 failures** post-push; `db:push` applied `20260733000000`; `db:types` reconciled. Closes the last read-leak the lifecycle audit found тАФ `photo_markups` was still role-level (cross-project). **Migration `20260733000000`:** recreates `can_see_photo_log(uuid)` (dropped in U3's revert) + adds `photo_markup_tombstone_target_ok(uuid,uuid)` тАФ a SECURITY DEFINER helper that performs the tombstone-target self-read (bypassing RLS, `auth.uid()` still the caller so the creator-pin holds). `photo_markups` SELECT тЖТ `can_see_photo_log`; INSERT keeps the content/own-tombstone rule but the tombstone branch now calls the helper instead of an inline `EXISTS (select тАж from photo_markups тАж)`, so the policy no longer self-joins the table тЖТ **no 42P17** (the U3 failure mode). Role list kept (coordinator read-only). **pgTAP file 74** (plan 12): both helpers exist + secdef, SELECT/INSERT wiring, and behaviourally the **exact content+tombstone INSERT that recursed in U3 now `lives_ok`** for a member, non-member sees 0 + INSERT denied, visitor sees 0. **Existing `31-photo-markups` (the comprehensive markup insert/tombstone/current-view suite) passes under the scoped policies** (its users are members via the U1 seed) тАФ strong real-world coverage that the recursion is gone and the member path is intact. **Lesson applied:** the pr_attachment_tombstone_target_ok pattern (definer helper for a self-referential append-only policy) is the canonical fix whenever such a table gets a function-based SELECT policy. **ADR 0056 "full isolation" is now actually complete** across all project-scoped tables (projects, work_packages, deliverables, photo_logs, approvals, purchase_requests, reports, labor_logs, work_package_dependencies, photo_markups); the only remaining write-side note is the labor RPCs (log_labor_day/correct_labor_log) gate on role + WP-status but not membership тАФ residual defense-in-depth (UI is read-locked for non-members), recorded, not exploitable.

## Spec 145 тАФ lock new work on a completed project (warranty-aware) (2026-06-18)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-18.** lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **1100 unit** ┬╖ green; **full pgTAP suite 76 files / 1521 asserts, 0 failures** post-push; `db:push` applied `20260735000000`; `db:types` reconciled. Operator decision: a project locks once completed тАФ **caveat:** completion тЙа full closure (client retains a warranty %, Buildall 5% for a year; defects surface in that window), so the lock blocks NEW work but must NOT block warranty defect-rework. **Enforcement = a `BEFORE INSERT` trigger on `work_packages`** (`work_packages_block_insert_on_closed_project`, raises `P0002`) gated by `project_is_open(uuid)` (status in active/on_hold) тАФ **one chokepoint** over every WP-creation path (manual/template/copy/CSV) without re-typing the 3 creation RPCs, and **INSERT-only** so spec-144 reopen-to-rework (an UPDATE) + the rework WP's capture/labor/approval cycle keep working on a completed project (the warranty carve-out falls out for free; gates on WP status, not project status). The **project record stays editable** (status тЖТ active to reopen the project; record retention notes in settings). **Actions** map `P0002` тЖТ "р╣Вр╕Др╕гр╕Зр╕Бр╕▓р╕гр╕Щр╕╡р╣Йр╕Ыр╕┤р╕Фр╣Бр╕ер╣Йр╕з р╣Ар╕Ыр╕┤р╕Фр╣Вр╕Др╕гр╕Зр╕Бр╕▓р╕гр╕Бр╣Ир╕нр╕ЩтАж" (createWorkPackage/copyWorkPackages/applyWpTemplate/importWorkPackagesCsv). **UI (project page):** added `status` to the project select + `projectOpen`; when closed, hides the seeding controls + onboarding checklist and shows a lock banner pointing to settings. **pgTAP file 76** (plan 11): helper truth table, direct-insert + all 3 RPCs blocked on a completed project (P0002), create still works on active, **reopen-for-defect still works on a completed project (warranty)**; fixtures seed WPs while active then flip to completed (so the seed doesn't trip the trigger). **Verified-by-checklist** (DB lock pgTAP'd; UI gate + action mapping are thin glue over the tested DB behavior). **Out of scope (deliberate):** retention %/warranty billing тАФ a finance feature the app resists (status-only at most, per ceo-review); not built. **Project lifecycle now complete:** active/on_hold (full edit) тЖТ completed (locked for new work; warranty: defects reopen individual WPs to rework тЖТ fix тЖТ re-approve) тЖТ archived; reopen the project via statusтЖТactive. **Audit-found project-status gap closed.**

## Spec 169 тАФ bottom tabs (+ hub strip) are first-layer destinations (2026-06-21)

Status: **SHIPPED тАФ 2026-06-21.** App-only, **no migration / no route / no role-set change** (nav behaviour). lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **unit green (nav suites 71; +1 TDD)** ┬╖ `pnpm build` green. Operator: _"Hitting the menu button should take users back to the top of the sitemap тАж all the tabs on the bottom of screen must be treated as first layer."_ **Root cause:** `BottomTabBar` rendered the **active** tab as an inert `<span>` (only inactive tabs were `<Link>`s), so on a sub-page (e.g. `/projects/[id]/...`) the section's own tab (р╣Вр╕Др╕гр╕Зр╕Бр╕▓р╕г) was active = **not tappable** тЖТ no one-tap way back to the section root (`/projects`, the first layer). **Fix:** render **every** tab as a `<Link>` to its root; the active one keeps its identity via `aria-current="page"` + the indicator bar + `text-action`/bold (active detection unchanged тАФ longest-prefix still lights exactly one). A tap on the active tab now returns to the first layer. **Extended to `HubNav`** (the desktop `sm:` strip the codebase keeps mirrored with the bottom bar тАФ same inert-`<span>` current item тЖТ same dead tab on a cloud PC; operator is a desktop user, so parity matters): current item is now a `<Link aria-current="page">` with the underline/`font-semibold` style. **Tests (path b):** `bottom-tab-bar.test.tsx` тАФ new test pins the active tab is a tappable `<a href=root>` on a deep `/projects/[id]/work-packages/[id]` path; the PM active tab (р╕гр╕нр╕Хр╕гр╕зр╕И on /review) is a link to /review; `hub-nav.test.tsx` тАФ every item is a link, current carries `aria-current` (was: span). Both updated the prior "active renders as a span, not a link" pins. **Scope note:** detail screens that deliberately hide the bottom bar (WP detail's thumb capture bar) are unchanged тАФ this only changes how the bar behaves where it already renders. **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated routes; the nav components are unit-pinned; build green; operator on-device = acceptance). Nova "external" now reads the **worker's** `dc_arrangement='temporary'` instead of the contractor party's `contractor_subtype='dc_temporary'`. CREATE OR REPLACE (signatures unchanged тЖТ grants preserved) the two functions that read the rule: `distribute_project_coins` (external тЖТ flat external_factor weight, else level weight) + `coin_unvested_balance` (external lock тАФ whole balance unvested). pgTAP 106 (distribution) + 108 (vesting) repointed: the external DC fixture is marked `update workers set dc_arrangement='temporary'` (keyed on the holdover dc_temporary contractor); assertions unchanged. The contracts-UI `dc_temporary` subtype labels (/contacts/dc) are untouched тАФ they're the party subtype display, cleaned up in U5. **NEXT:** U3 dc_paymentsтЖТworker.

## Spec 175 тАФ item catalog (on-site storage / inventory foundation), U1 (2026-06-22)

Status: **U1 SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-22.** lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **vitest 1366 (206 files; +1 TDD: catalog-list)** ┬╖ **db:test 121 files / 2311 / 0** ┬╖ `pnpm build` green; db:push applied `20260801000000`; db:types regenerated. First unit of the on-site **storage-unit / inventory** feature (design in `docs/inventory-store/README.md`): the store is a transfer-pricing BU with three flows (Supply Plan / Stock-In / р╣Ар╕Ър╕┤р╕Б), staged **cost-first**; everything downstream keys on one **item identity**, which the per-site spreadsheet can't provide. **U1 builds that item master тАФ read-only + seeded.** **Migration `20260801000000`:** new enum `item_category` (12 codes) + `catalog_items` (id, category, base_item, spec_attrs, unit text, stockable, note, is_active, created_at) тАФ reference data, **read-only to authenticated** (RLS enable; revoke anon+authenticated; grant select authenticated; SELECT policy `using(true)`; **no write policy** тЖТ seeded by migration, the `wp_templates` posture spec 142). **Unique identity** index on `(base_item, coalesce(spec_attrs,''))` = the anti-drift guard the sheet lacked. **Seeded 71 deduped items** from the operator's previous-site purchase sheet (`docs/inventory-store/seed-catalog.csv`); **17 `stockable=false`** (made-to-length roofing CC/760+р╕Др╕гр╕нр╕Ъ, fire doors, stainless fab, engineered Aqua tanks тЖТ direct-to-WP, never inventoried). **Units stored as text reusing `COMMON_UNITS`** (spec 16 doctrine: units are client-side text, NOT a DB table тАФ the course-correction from the original two-table design) тАФ normalised р╕Бр╕Б.тЖТр╕Бр╕┤р╣Вр╕ер╕Бр╕гр╕▒р╕б, р╕б.тЖТр╣Ар╕бр╕Хр╕г; non-stock lines (freight/service/VAT/WHT) excluded. **No prices** (price is not item identity; real cost comes from receipts later). **Page `/catalog`:** server component, `requireRole(BACK_OFFICE_ROLES)` (pm/super/procurement/director тАФ the back-office curators, mirroring the suppliers master), settings drill-down (DetailHeaderтЖТ/settings + BottomTabBar, no HubNav). `CatalogList` (pure presentational) groups by category in **enum order** (iterates the ITEM_CATEGORY_LABEL key order), each row base_item┬╖spec┬╖unit + a **р╣Ар╕Бр╣Зр╕Ър╕кр╕Хр╣Кр╕нр╕Б / р╕кр╕▒р╣Ир╕Зр╕Хр╕гр╕Зр╣Ар╕Вр╣Йр╕▓р╕Зр╕▓р╕Щ** badge; empty state. **Labels (SSOT, labels.ts):** `CATALOG_LABEL`=р╕Чр╕░р╣Ар╕Ър╕╡р╕вр╕Щр╕зр╕▒р╕кр╕Фр╕╕, `ITEM_CATEGORY_LABEL` (12), `CATALOG_STOCKABLE_LABEL`/`CATALOG_NON_STOCKABLE_LABEL`. **Nav:** р╕Чр╕░р╣Ар╕Ър╕╡р╕вр╕Щр╕зр╕▒р╕кр╕Фр╕╕ door (Package icon) in the procurement block + isManager master-data block of `/settings`; `/catalog` added to the р╕Хр╕▒р╣Йр╕Зр╕Др╣Ир╕▓ tab `match`. **Tests:** `catalog-list.test.tsx` (5: section per present category, **enum order not input order**, item name/spec/unit, stockable badge counts, empty state); pgTAP `119-item-catalog` (10: table/RLS, enum 12-label pin, anon-deny + auth-allow grants, **unique-identity reject (23505)**, seed present + known item + stockable & non-stockable exist). **Three completeness guards updated (the repo's anti-drift net):** `nav-back-affordance` STATIC_DETAIL (classify `catalog`), `feature-components-structure` ALLOWED_DOMAINS (new `catalog` domain folder), `bottom-tab-bar` р╕Хр╕▒р╣Йр╕Зр╕Др╣Ир╕▓ match. **Lessons:** the codebase already had a units vocabulary (`src/lib/purchasing/units.ts`) тАФ reused it as text rather than inventing an `item_units` table (CLAUDE.md: don't swap the established approach); adding a `features/<domain>/` folder trips the `feature-components-structure` allowlist (third anti-drift guard, alongside nav-back-affordance + the tab match). **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated page тЖТ /login in preview; Out of scope here: store entity, Stock-In, р╣Ар╕Ър╕┤р╕Б/Issue, custody handshake, sell-rate/margin layer.

Replace + remove; **old objects retained on replace** (keep-originals doctrine [[ai-driven-direction-keep-images]]). Mounted on the `EditCatalogItem` sheet (image attaches on EDIT тАФ the item must exist for its storage path; matches "existing list"). **Display:** the page mints 120s signed URLs via **`mintSignedUrls(CATALOG_IMAGES_BUCKET, тАж)`** (spec-65 shared core) for items with `image_path` тЖТ `thumbnailUrl` on `CatalogItem` тЖТ `CatalogList` renders a 40px thumbnail; placeholder icon when empty. **Actions** `setCatalogItemImage`: `requireRole(BACK_OFFICE_ROLES)`, UUID-guard, empty path тЖТ clear, map `42501`/`22023`. **Tests:** `catalog-image-control.test.tsx` (3: downscaleтЖТuploadтЖТrecordтЖТrefresh w/ path `^{id}/тАж\.jpeg$`, removeтЖТnull, reject-non-image) + pgTAP `122-catalog-item-image` (10). **`<img>` for signed URLs** (same as `ZoomablePhoto`) with an eslint-disable for `@next/next/no-img-element`. **Typecheck caught** `exactOptionalPropertyTypes`: pass `item.thumbnailUrl ?? null` (optional field тЖТ can't hand an explicit `undefined` to a `?: string | null` prop). **Verified-by-checklist** (browser-upload seam is review/operator-phone verified per spec-34 precedent; control unit-pinned, RPC+bucket pgTAP'd). **Decision:** single current image (Option A) + retained old blobs honours keep-images without an append-only table; a `catalog_item_images` history table stays an additive later option. **NEXT:** Phase 2 тАФ the **Supply Plan** (the PM-accuracy engine). The item master is now view/add/edit/deactivate/image тАФ feature-complete as a catalog.

## Spec 176 тАФ Supply Plan, U3: submit + PD approve/reject (2026-06-22)

Status: **U3 SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-22.** lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **vitest 1388 (210 files; +2: supply-plan-manager lifecycle)** ┬╖ **db:test 127 files / 2391 / 0** (file 178, 17 asserts) ┬╖ `pnpm build` green; db:push applied `20260807000000`; db:types regenerated (+3). The plan lifecycle + freeze. **Lifecycle:** `draft тЖТ(PM submit)тЖТ submitted тЖТ(PD approve)тЖТ approved [FROZEN]` / `тЖТ(PD reject)тЖТ rejected тЖТ(PM revises+resubmits)`. **Separation of duties:** planner tier (pm/super/director) SUBMITS; only the approver tier (`project_director`/`super_admin`) APPROVES/REJECTS тАФ a plain PM cannot approve its own plan (pgTAP-pinned: PM approve тЖТ 42501). **Migration `20260807`:** `submit_supply_plan` (planner; draft|rejectedтЖТsubmitted, sets submitted_at), `approve_supply_plan` (PD/super; submittedтЖТapproved, sets approved_by/at), `reject_supply_plan` (PD/super; submittedтЖТrejected); all SECURITY DEFINER + `can_see_project` + status-guard (wrong status тЖТ 22023), anon-revoked. **CREATE OR REPLACE `add_supply_plan_line` + `remove_supply_plan_line`** to widen the edit gate `draft тЖТ draft|rejected` (a rejected plan is revisable) тАФ same signatures so grants preserved (anon stays revoked; no pgTAP signature-pin break). **`SupplyPlanManager`:** `editable` includes `rejected`; header action group by state/role тАФ **р╕кр╣Ир╕Зр╕нр╕Щр╕╕р╕бр╕▒р╕Хр╕┤** (planner, draft/rejected), **р╕нр╕Щр╕╕р╕бр╕▒р╕Хр╕┤/р╕Хр╕╡р╕Бр╕ер╕▒р╕Ъ** (approver, submitted), **р╕гр╕нр╕нр╕Щр╕╕р╕бр╕▒р╕Хр╕┤** text (non-approver, submitted), frozen when approved. Page passes `planId` + `canApprove` (`ctx.role` director/super). **Actions** `submitPlan`/`approvePlan`/`rejectPlan`: getActionUser + RPC + map 42501/22023 + revalidatePath. **Tests:** `supply-plan-manager.test.tsx` (+3: submit, approve+reject, non-approver read-only) + pgTAP `178-supply-plan-lifecycle` (17: submit/approve/reject transitions, PMтЙаapprover 42501, approved-frozen, rejected-editable-again, wrong-status 22023, visitor 42501). **NEXT:** U4 reactive-PR reason codes (tag scramble-orders; `unplanned-miss` dings PM), U5 measurement (planned vs reactive).

## Spec 176 тАФ Supply Plan, U4: reactive-PR reason codes (2026-06-22)

Status: **U4 SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-22.** lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **vitest 212 files / 1399 (+53: reason-code validators + 2 form tests + reason-module pins)** ┬╖ **db:test 128 files / 2406 / 0** (file 179, 16 asserts; file 33 + 91 updated) ┬╖ `pnpm build` green; db:push applied `20260808000000` + `20260808000100`; db:types regenerated. Operator-locked (AskUserQuestion): (1) the 5-code taxonomy `unplanned_miss`/`rework`/`breakage`/`scope_change`/`unforeseeable` тАФ **only `unplanned_miss` counts against the PM**; (2) **required on every PR**; (3) **both create paths** (the `/requests` form + the WP-detail on-site quick-record). **Design (spec 176 ┬зU4):** new enum `purchase_request_reason_code` + nullable `purchase_requests.reason_code` (NO default тАФ legacy rows stay null = pre-feature/unscored; required-ness on the WRITE paths, not a column NOT NULL or DB CHECK тАФ matches the `priority`/`needed_by` requester-field posture, ADR 0026); additive `grant insert (reason_code)` (column-scoped grant, spec 33); **insert RLS untouched** (pins 70/73/91/115 + the 64 owner-role fixtures stay green). Form path: `validateCreatePurchaseRequest` gains a required `reasonCode` (checked LAST so existing earlier-field error cases keep their message) + `createPurchaseRequest` inserts `reason_code` + a required reason `<select>` on `PurchaseRequestForm`. Site path: `validateSitePurchase` + `recordSitePurchase` + a required reason `<select>` on `SitePurchaseForm`. Shared `src/lib/purchasing/reason-code.ts` (type + list + guard) + `PURCHASE_REQUEST_REASON_CODE_LABEL` (р╕зр╕▓р╕Зр╣Бр╕Ьр╕Щр╕Хр╕Бр╕лр╕ер╣Ир╕Щ/р╕Зр╕▓р╕Щр╣Бр╕Бр╣Йр╣Др╕В/р╕Вр╕нр╕Зр╕Кр╕│р╕гр╕╕р╕Ф┬╖р╣Ар╕кр╕╡р╕вр╕лр╕▓р╕в/р╕Вр╕нр╕Ър╣Ар╕Вр╕Хр╕Зр╕▓р╕Щр╣Ар╕Ыр╕ер╕╡р╣Ир╕вр╕Щ/р╣Ар╕лр╕Хр╕╕р╕кр╕╕р╕Фр╕зр╕┤р╕кр╕▒р╕в). **Out of scope (тЖТU5):** card/list display + planned-vs-reactive aggregation (the column carries the tag for U5 to read). **Migrations split into TWO:** `20260808000000` = enum + column + insert grant; `20260808000100` = `record_site_purchase` DROP+CREATE. **TWO traps caught by db:push/db:test + fixed forward тЖТ [[prc-ops-db-migration-lessons]]:** (1) **OVERLOAD** тАФ I sourced the RPC body from migration file `20260630000100` (5-arg) but the LIVE function was the **7-arg VAT version** (`20260701000200` added `p_vat_rate`); my first `record_site_purchase` create made a vat-LESS duplicate (would regress VAT) instead of replacing it. Fix: drop the real `(тАж,numeric,numeric)` + create the **7-arg** `(uuid,text,numeric,text,reason_code,numeric,numeric)` with reason BEFORE the defaulted amount/vat, VAT preserved; queried `pg_proc` to confirm a single signature; made mig 100 self-dropping (drops its own 7-arg too) so a repair+repush is idempotent. (2) **project_director ride-along** тАФ the reconstructed pre-152 body dropped `project_director` from the gate тЖТ **pgTAP file 91** ("no PM-gated RPC left without project_director") went RED; re-added it. Plus a pgTAP UUID hex-length slip in 179 (13-char final group). **The meta-lesson: reconstruct a definer RPC body from the LIVE `pg_get_functiondef`/`pg_proc`, never an old migration file.** **Tests:** pgTAP 179 + `validate-purchase-request`/`validate-site-purchase` (+reason cases) + `purchase-request-form-reason` + `site-purchase-form-reason`. **NEXT:** U5 measurement (planned `supply_plan_lines` vs reactive `unplanned_miss` PRs, per project/WP/PM тАФ the PM-accuracy number).

## Spec 176 тАФ Supply Plan, U5: measurement (PM-accuracy) (2026-06-22)

Status: **U5 SHIPPED to prod тАФ 2026-06-22.** lint ┬╖ typecheck ┬╖ **vitest 213 files / 1402 (+3: supply-plan-accuracy)** ┬╖ **db:test 129 files / 2421 / 0** (file 180, 15 asserts) ┬╖ `pnpm build` green; db:push applied `20260808000200`; db:types regenerated. **Spec 176 arc COMPLETE.** The payoff: surface planned vs reactive so the operator sees how well a PM planned. Migration `20260808000200` (808000000/100 were U4), pgTAP `180`. **Design (spec 176 ┬зU5):** PRs carry `work_package_id` + free-text item (no `catalog_item_id`) тЖТ can only measure count-based PER WP (no PRтЖФplan-line item match). **RPC `supply_plan_accuracy(p_project_id)`** SECURITY DEFINER, planner tier (incl. project_director per file-91 pin) + `can_see_project` (unknownтЖТ22023); returns a TABLE one row per WP (or null=site-general) with a plan line OR a PR: `planned_lines`, `planned_qty`, `unplanned_miss`, `fair_reactive` (rework/breakage/scope_change/unforeseeable), `untagged` (null reason). FULL OUTER JOIN of per-WP planned + per-WP PR aggregates (PRsтЖТproject via `work_packages.project_id`), worst-offender first. ALL PR statuses count (status-filter = flagged refinement). **Surface:** read-only `SupplyPlanAccuracy` server component on `/projects/[id]/supply-plan` тАФ project totals (planned ┬╖ unplanned_miss HIGHLIGHTED ┬╖ fair ┬╖ untagged) + per-WP table (site-general = "р╕Чр╕▒р╣Йр╕Зр╣Вр╕Др╕гр╕Зр╕Бр╕▓р╕г"). **Per-PM:** per-project number = per-PM-per-project (plan has created_by); cross-project roll-up = flagged follow-up, NOT built. **Tests:** pgTAP 180 + `supply-plan-accuracy.test.tsx`. **Lesson (caught by db:test):** the plan-line unique index is `(plan, item, coalesce(wp, sentinel))` тЖТ two lines on the SAME WP need TWO catalog items; my first fixture used one item and asserted 2 lines (impossible) тАФ the RPC was correct, the fixture wrong. **Spec 176 (Supply Plan) COMPLETE: U1 data тЖТ U2 planning UI тЖТ U3 submit/approve freeze тЖТ U4 reactive reason codes тЖТ U5 PM-accuracy measure. NEXT (storage arc Phase 3):** store + stock-in at cost (р╕гр╕▒р╕Ър╣Ар╕Вр╣Йр╕▓ тЖТ store buys from supplier; reuse deliveries spec 135).
